# C4 Autonomous Queue v10 — Web hook test expansion

24h autonomous run that adds vitest tests to web/src/lib/use-* hooks not yet covered. The Meetings (19/19), ui-primitives (6/6), and most Sessions/Specialists/Chat/Attach hooks are already done; this queue tackles the remaining domains (Wiki, Workflow, Autonomous, Auth, Audit, generic) and the leftover Specialists pair.

## Tasks

|---|------|--------|--------|
| 11.10 | Wiki hooks vitest | done | Add vitest tests for these 4 web hooks: web/src/lib/use-wiki-search.ts, web/src/lib/use-wiki-page.ts, web/src/lib/use-wiki-bulk-publish.ts, web/src/lib/use-wiki-reopen.ts. Branch c4/auto-wiki. Worker auto-w1. Pattern: see web/src/lib/use-meeting-create.test.ts and use-meetings-search.test.ts. For each hook cover idle initial state, every setter / callback exposed in return, validation paths that reject without fetch, happy-path REST verifying body shape + path + encodeURIComponent on any id, server-error path, busy slot via release-gate Promise pattern, cross-selection / open=false reset effects. Run npm --prefix /root/c4-worktree-auto-w1/web test (symlink web/node_modules to /root/c4/web/node_modules first if needed — gitignored) and confirm ALL passing. Then update /root/c4/CHANGELOG.md (## [1.11.25] entry above 1.11.24 with file + case count), bump /root/c4/package.json (1.11.24 to 1.11.25) and the two version lines in /root/c4/package-lock.json. Commit on this branch with a descriptive message. DO NOT push and DO NOT merge — manager handles. Touch only the new test files + CHANGELOG + package.json + package-lock.json — work in worktree, never edit /root/c4/web/* directly. |

## Operating rules

- One task at a time, throttleMs (10 minutes) between dispatches.
- Worker uses the assigned branch; commit must stay on that branch (no push from worker).
- Manager (c4-mgr-auto) verifies each commit, fast-forwards into main, pushes to origin via SSH.
- Circuit breaker: 3 consecutive failures stop the loop until manual resume (c4 autonomous resume).
- Escalation: any halt surfaces in /api/autonomous/escalations and on the Web UI Autonomous tab.

Bump 1.11.91. Shipped: src/daemon-checkpoint.js (new) exports CHECKPOINT_GRACE_MS=30_000, DEFAULT_VERSION, checkpointDir, buildCheckpointPayload, writeCheckpoint (atomic write — stages to `<os.tmpdir()>/<name>.<pid>.json.tmp` then renames into `<projectRoot>/.c4/checkpoints/<name>.json`, mkdir recursive on the destination), and shutdownWorkers (enumerate workers -> write checkpoint -> SIGTERM live procs -> poll every 250ms until the map empties or graceMs elapses -> SIGKILL any survivor -> emit per-worker log lines `graceful exit` / `force-killed after Ns`). All sequencing functions accept DI hooks (now / delay / kill / isAlive / writeCheckpoint / log / fs / tmpDir) so the test suite drives the poll loop without sleeping. src/daemon.js `_gracefulShutdown` is now async + idempotent (a re-entry guard short-circuits a second SIGINT/SIGTERM during shutdown); it calls `await daemonCheckpoint.shutdownWorkers(manager.workers.values(), { projectRoot, version: manager._daemonVersion, log })` in place of `manager.closeAll()`, so worktrees and branches are preserved across daemon stops. uncaughtException is intentionally NOT wired to this path -- the module documents `skipCheckpoint:true` for any future emergency-stop branch so an inconsistent process state never writes a misleading checkpoint. Checkpoint payload schema matches the v1.11.91 contract: { name, branch, worktree, pid, target, tier (defaults to "worker"), lastTask: { summary, timestamp } \| null, stoppedAt, version }. lastTask pulls from worker._taskText (first line, max 200 chars) and worker._taskStartedAt; null when the worker never received a task. tests/daemon-checkpoint.test.js (new, 20 cases, node:test) covers: payload schema, pretty-printed JSON on disk, atomic tmp-then-rename, mkdir recursive, missing _taskText, summary truncation + first-line-only, tier/target defaults, name-required guard, real-fs end-to-end under os.mkdtempSync, shutdownWorkers walks every worker + writes checkpoint each, SIGTERMs every live worker, resolves early on graceful exit, escalates SIGKILL after graceMs, per-worker log lines (graceful exit / force-killed after Ns), skipCheckpoint=true bypass (uncaughtException contract), checkpoint path on each result entry, kill-error outcome, writeCheckpoint failure does not abort the pass, CHECKPOINT_GRACE_MS export = 30_000, and a textual ordering assertion that daemon.js calls shutdownWorkers BEFORE server.close() so the listening socket closes last. | 11.85 | Performance: daemon hot paths | partial | Profile `c4 list` and `c4 autonomous status` end-to-end. Add in-memory cache with 2s TTL for c4 list response and worker status snapshots. Target: c4 list p50 latency < 50ms. Add a perf test in src/daemon/perf.test.js. Branch c4/auto-perf-daemon. Worker auto-w76 (auto-w72 slot reused). Bump 1.11.103. Shipped: new `src/cache-ttl.js` exporting `createCache({ ttlMs })` with `get` / `set` / `invalidate(key?)` / `getOrCompute(key, asyncCompute)`. `getOrCompute` returns cached values within TTL, otherwise runs the compute once and stores the result; concurrent callers during a pending compute share the same Promise (stampede protection); rejected computes clear the in-flight slot so the next call retries; clock is injectable for deterministic test expiry. Two daemon singletons: `cacheList = createCache({ ttlMs: 2000 })` wraps the `/api/list` handler body via `cacheList.getOrCompute('list', async () => ...)`; `cacheAutoStatus = createCache({ ttlMs: 2000 })` wraps `/api/autonomous/status` the same way. Invalidation hooks at every state-change site: `cacheList.invalidate('list')` on `/create` success and `/close` success; `cacheAutoStatus.invalidate('status')` on `/autonomous/pause`, `/autonomous/resume`, and `/autonomous/tick`. Profiling (`tools/profile-daemon-endpoints.js`, 100 iterations per N): list() p50 0.18 ms at N=10, 0.37 ms at N=30, 0.58 ms at N=50 -- well under the 50 ms target even before caching. workerMetrics.sample is the dominant slice (two `fs.readFileSync` calls into `/proc/<pid>/{status,stat}` per worker, scales linearly with N); JSON.stringify is small but real (p50 0.03 ms at N=30, 0.05 ms at N=50); per-worker intervention / failure-hint computation is already memoized. New `tests/cache-ttl.test.js` 13 cases / 4 suites: get / set basics + missing-key undefined, defaults to 2000 ms, key independence, getOrCompute TTL freshness window, exact-boundary expiry, two-caller stampede sharing one Promise, rejected-compute cleanup so the next call retries, post-resolve cache hit, `invalidate(key)` drops one entry, `invalidate()` with no arg clears every entry, `invalidate` forcing the next call to recompute. `web/package.json` 1.11.102 -> 1.11.103. CHANGELOG `[1.11.103]` covers findings + cache contract + invalidation points. Verification: `node --test tests/cache-ttl.test.js` 13/13 pass; `node -c src/daemon.js` clean. Deferred to follow-up: `tests/daemon-perf.test.js` (supertest-based perf test asserting cache hit < 5 ms, p50 across 100 sequential calls < 5000 ms wall, invalidation paths on /create+/close and /autonomous/{tick,pause,resume}) -- the deliverable's p50 target is already comfortably met by the un-cached baseline and the cache reduces per-call cost to a `Map.get` once the first compute lands, but pinning that as a regression gate is the remaining piece. |

| 11.228 | UI: lazy-route prefetch | done | SHIPPED v1.11.246 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto, merged via --no-ff). web/src/lib/route-prefetch.ts (99 lines): prefetch(loader) is a WeakMap-cached warm-up that calls a () => import(...) once per loader identity, swallows rejections + drops the cache entry so a retry is possible, no-ops under SSR, and ignores non-thenable return values + synchronous throws defensively. prefetchHandlers(loader) returns the canonical { onMouseEnter, onFocus, onTouchStart } triple so a consumer can spread the wiring onto a nav button without re-deriving it. TouchStart fires alongside mouse/focus signals because a touch user never sees mouseenter; firing on press-down warms the chunk during the ~150ms before synthetic-click delivery. web/src/lib/route-loaders.ts (52 lines): single source of truth for the 10 top-level view loaders so the prefetch path and the React.lazy(...) boundaries in App.tsx target the same module URLs (the bundler de-dupes the underlying chunk fetch, and the prefetch cache stays keyed by stable function identity -- an arrow defined inside a render would defeat the WeakMap after every re-render, so the loaders are exported once at module scope). Adoption: web/src/components/ui/tabs.tsx -- primitive grows optional onPrefetch?: (value: string) => void; each tab button wires onMouseEnter + onFocus + onTouchStart to fire with the tab's value, skipping the already-active tab and disabled rows; existing onChange semantics unchanged. web/src/components/layout/TopTabs.tsx -- routes the new prop to prefetch(getTopViewLoader(value)) so a hover/focus/touchstart on any sibling tab warms the lazy chunk before the click commits. web/src/components/ui/dropdown-menu.tsx -- DropdownMenuItem gains optional onPrefetch; the rendered <button> wires it to the existing mouseenter/focus path (disabled rows skip). web/src/components/AccountMenu.tsx -- the Preferences row now warms the SettingsView chunk on hover/focus via the shared SETTINGS_LOADER export. Hook accepts a map of sequence -> handler, listens on window for plain-letter keydowns, buffers each press, fires on exact match. 1500ms inactivity timer expires the buffer (timeoutMs option overrides). Two new modules give every animation surface a single source of truth: web/src/styles/motion.css (100 lines) -- CSS custom properties for the canonical motion scale: --motion-duration-{instant 80, fast 150, normal 200, slow 300, deliberate 500}ms; --motion-ease-{standard, out, in, emphasized} (Material 3 vocabulary, with standard = cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)); two spring presets --motion-spring-snappy (~5% overshoot via cubic-bezier(0.2, 0.8, 0.2, 1.05) for tooltips/toasts) + --motion-spring-soft (~15% overshoot via cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1) for hero motion). Required because JS callers like Toast's style.transition string cannot read CSS variables synchronously. (2) Drawer -- transition-transform utility now stacks motion-duration-normal motion-ease-standard so Drawer moves on the same curve as Dialog/Popover (Tailwind's default 150ms/ease-in-out was wrong for a large surface). (3) Dialog -- already routed through motionClass('fadeIn'/'scaleIn') in lib/motion.ts; lib doc-comment updated to point at the central tokens so Tailwind duration classes (duration-150/duration-200) read as the fast/normal steps. Hook is deliberately decoupled from the <Table> primitive: any surface (canonical data table, virtualized list, list of cards) can persist its sort by feeding the value into a comparator -- the <Table> primitive itself stays byte-identical (already controlled). Adoption at 2 sites: (1) TokenUsage.tsx PerTaskTable -- worker/total/input/output columns now sortable (task text column stays unsortable since free-text doesn't sort meaningfully), default sort = total desc (operator's most common question is which task burned the most tokens this window), persisted to c4:table-sort:token-usage-per-task, pure perTaskComparator exported with 9 vitest cases covering all 4 keys + asc/desc + null coercion + total-from-input+output fallback + stability; sort runs before pagination via useMemo so the page slice reflects the chosen ordering. 33/33 existing TokenUsage.test.tsx cases still pass. (2) HistoryView.tsx sidebar virtualized list -- new Select dropdown (Last task / Name / Task count) + direction toggle button (ArrowUpAZ/ArrowDownAZ icons with aria-label that swaps with direction), default sort = lastTaskAt desc (matches the prior implicit order so first-load DOM is byte-identical), persisted to c4:table-sort:history-sidebar, pure historySidebarComparator exported with 8 vitest cases including the deliberate quirk that null lastTaskAt entries sort to the end regardless of direction so never-active workers don't crowd the operator's view. Sort applies after the search-query filter so changing sort never changes which rows match the search. 43/43 existing HistoryView.test.tsx cases still pass. exactOptionalPropertyTypes: true is on in the worktree's tsconfig so the new code spreads sortKey/sortDir props only when defined ({...(sortKey ? { sortKey } : {})}) instead of passing undefined; pre-existing failures (Templates / Swarm / Workspaces / Validation) are unchanged and out of scope. | 11.250 | UI: kbd shortcut chip | done | SHIPPED v1.11.268 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto, merged via --no-ff). The Kbd primitive already had children + keys render modes; this release adds a third mode with platform-aware modifier glyph mapping plus exported helpers. New combo: string prop parses shortcut strings like "Mod+K" / "Ctrl+Shift+P" / "Shift+/" into a per-platform sequence of glyphs. Modifier tokens flip to Mac glyphs on mac (Cmd -> ⌘ U+2318, Shift -> ⇧ U+21E7, Alt / Option -> ⌥ U+2325, Ctrl -> ⌃ U+2303) and stay verbatim on Windows / Linux. The `Mod` alias is the canonical "platform meta" token (mac: ⌘, other: Ctrl) so shortcut authors can write one combo and the right glyph renders everywhere. Mac also flips Enter / Backspace / Esc / Tab / Space / arrow keys to their HIG glyphs (↵ ⌫ ⎋ ⇥ ␣ ↑↓←→). Non-modifier keys (letters / digits / "/" / "?") stay literal. Mac defaults to NO inter-chip separator (tight Apple HIG layout); non-mac defaults to " + "; callers can override via the existing separator prop. Exported helpers mapKey(token, platform) / parseCombo(combo, platform) / detectPlatform() with the detector reading navigator.userAgent + navigator.platform and returning 'mac' | 'other'; tests override per-call via the explicit platform prop. New data-platform="mac" | "other" attribute on the multi-key root wrapper for e2e selectors. 15 new vitest cases (27/27 total) cover: combo + mac glyphs, combo + other verbatim, Mod alias both ways, 3-key combo, mac drops separator, non-mac keeps " + ", custom separator override, Alt/Option/Enter/Backspace/Esc/Tab/Space mac glyphs, non-modifier keys verbatim, parseCombo trim, data-platform attribute, detectPlatform smoke, combo wins over keys. Adopted at CommandPalette.tsx: the shortcut chip now uses <Kbd combo={cmd.shortcut} /> so mac operators see ⌘K instead of "Mod+K" and non-mac stays "Ctrl + K"; 35/35 CommandPalette tests pass. KeyboardShortcutsModal.tsx continues to use the legacy literal-children path (<Kbd>{row.keys}</Kbd>) so its 47 pre-existing test assertions (which match the concatenated string text like "Ctrl+F") stay green; future work can migrate the Modal once those assertions restructure around per-chip selectors. AccountMenu + HelpDrawer already use Kbd in single-key mode (<Kbd>?</Kbd>) so no change is needed there. | 11.396 | UI: snapshot diff viewer | done | SHIPPED v1.11.414 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/snapshot-diff.tsx` ships `<SnapshotDiff>` -- side-by-side or unified text diff renderer with line numbers, fold unchanged hunks, prev/next change navigation, optional renderText hook for syntax highlighting. Owns: pure LCS-based line diff `computeLineDiff(before, after) -> DiffLine[]` (`{ type: 'equal'|'add'|'remove', oldLineNumber, newLineNumber, text }`; empty strings yield `[]` not `['']`); change-block grouping `findDiffChangeBlocks(lines) -> {startIndex, endIndex}[]` (consecutive non-equal runs = one block, which is the navigation unit); hunk grouping `groupDiffHunks(lines, contextLines=3) -> DiffHunk[]` (folds equal runs > 2*contextLines, keeps contextLines anchor on each side of each change block, no-anchor edges collapse so an all-equal diff folds entirely); side-by-side row generator `pairSideBySide(lines)` (pairs consecutive remove + add into one row, excess goes to its own row with the opposite side null). Navigation: Prev/Next buttons in header (cycle through change blocks, wrap at ends); keyboard `n` / `Alt+ArrowDown` next, `p` / `Alt+ArrowUp` prev, plain Arrow keys fall through to scroll, Ctrl/Cmd+n/p no-op; counter shows `<idx+1> / <N>` ("1 / 2") or "0 / 0" when no changes (buttons disabled). Controlled `activeChangeIndex` + `onActiveChangeIndex(idx)` or uncontrolled `defaultActiveChangeIndex=0`; both modes fire onActiveChangeIndex. Fold rendering: one button per fold ("... <N> unchanged lines (click to expand)") with aria-label "Expand <N> unchanged lines"; per-hunk expand state (expanding one fold leaves others collapsed); `defaultExpandedFolds=true` mounts with everything expanded. Syntax highlighting NOT bundled -- pass `renderText: (text, language) => ReactNode` to plug in Prism/Highlight.js/Shiki; default renders plain monospace pre-wrap. ARIA: root `role="region"` + tabIndex=0 + aria-label; fold button + nav buttons all have descriptive aria-labels; data attrs throughout (data-section + data-mode + data-language + data-change-count + data-active-change-index on root; data-line-type + data-line-index + data-active per row; data-side + data-line-type on side-by-side cells; data-fold-id + data-fold-count on fold row). forwardRef forwarded to region root. 52 new test cases in snapshot-diff.test.tsx (7 computeLineDiff + 4 findDiffChangeBlocks + 5 groupDiffHunks + 5 pairSideBySide + 31 component); 52/52 pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented): bundled highlighter (use renderText), word/character-level intra-line diff, three-way merge diff, Patience/Myers-O(ND) algorithm (LCS is correct + simple for v1), side-by-side empty-row alignment across multi-line adds, copy/share-link buttons (belong in the audit host). New `web/src/components/ui/markdown-renderer.tsx` ships `<MarkdownRenderer>` -- a secure markdown-to-React renderer with URL sanitization, fenced-code routed through `<CodeBlock>` (11.379) for syntax highlighting, optional GFM checkbox lists, custom anchor click hook. Block grammar: ATX headings 1..6, fenced code (` ``` ` or ` ```lang `), blockquote (`> ` lines), horizontal rule (`---`/`***`/`___`), unordered list (`-`/`*`/`+`), ordered list (`1. `), checkbox list (`- [ ]`/`- [x]`/`[X]`), paragraph (blank-line separated). Inline grammar: `` `code` ``, `**bold**`, `*italic*`/`_italic_`, `~~strikethrough~~`, `[label](url)` with URL sanitization, bare `http(s):` autolink. URL sanitization via exported pure helper `safeUrl(url): string | null`: allows http/https/mailto/tel/relative-path/fragment/no-scheme-relative; blocks empty/whitespace/javascript:/data:/vbscript:/file:/any-unknown-scheme (safer fallback). When a `[label](url)` link sanitizes to null the anchor is dropped but the label remains as plain text. Override via `sanitizeUrl` prop to allow app schemes (e.g. `myapp://`). Anchor rendering: `linkTarget` (default '_blank') with `rel="noopener noreferrer"` auto-applied when blank, omitted for self; `onAnchorClick(href, event)` fires with SANITIZED href; raw URL preserved on `data-href-raw` attr for tests + analytics. Checkbox lists: contiguous `- [ ]`/`- [x]` runs render as `<input type="checkbox">` list; `data-checkbox-index` is FLAT across whole document for stable cross-list addressing; `data-checked` mirrors state; `onCheckboxChange(flatIdx, checked)` fires on toggle; read-only when no handler supplied; `enableCheckboxes={false}` collapses to plain ul with `data-checkbox-disabled="true"`. Code-block integration: fenced code blocks delegate to existing `<CodeBlock>` primitive (11.379) so the markdown renderer inherits syntax highlighting + copy button + line numbers + theme without duplicating logic; wrapper marked `data-section="markdown-code-block"` for test locality; `language` prop provides fallback for un-tagged fences. Pure helpers exported: `safeUrl(url)`, `parseMarkdownBlocks(source) -> MarkdownBlock[]`, type `MarkdownBlockType` union. ARIA: root `role="region"` + aria-label; checkbox inputs aria-labelled with item text; safe link rel-noopener-noreferrer when target=blank. Data attrs throughout (data-section + data-block-count on root; data-section + data-level per heading; data-checkbox-index + data-checked per checkbox-item; data-href-raw per link; data-section per inline-code/bold/italic/strike/autolink). forwardRef forwarded to root region. 52 new test cases in markdown-renderer.test.tsx (8 safeUrl + 11 parseMarkdownBlocks + 33 component); 52/52 pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented): GFM tables (pipe-table parsing non-trivial; follow-on), HTML pass-through (intentionally sanitized; raw HTML denied by omission), footnotes/definitions/reference-style links, image rendering (CORS + referrer-policy concerns; follow-on), math/LaTeX, smart-typography (curly quotes, em-dash), adoption sweep through existing pages (legacy lib/markdown.tsx continues to drive Plan + Morning until separate migration dispatch). Reference /root/c4/arps-design-system-v1/. Branch c4/auto-ui-markdown-renderer. Worker auto-w382. Bump 1.11.418. |
| 11.401 | UI: list-virtualizer primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.419 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/list-virtualizer.tsx` ships `<ListVirtualizer>` -- generalised virtual list with dynamic per-row heights, smooth scroll, sticky headers, keyboard navigation. Distinct from `<VirtualList>` (11.197, fixed-height) and `<VirtualTable>` (11.375, tabular). API: `items: ListVirtualizerItem<T>[]` (`{ id, data, type?: 'row'|'header', estimatedHeight?, disabled? }`); `renderItem(item, ctx)` slot; controlled-or-uncontrolled `activeIndex`; `stickyHeaders` flag; `scrollBehavior` default; `onEndReached` + `endReachedThreshold`; `enableKeyboardNav` toggle; imperative handle `{ scrollToIndex(idx, behavior?), scrollToTop(behavior?), getScrollTop() }`. Dynamic heights: ref-callback on every rendered row captures `getBoundingClientRect().height` on mount; measurement Map feeds back into cumulative offset array; stale measurements drop when items.length shrinks; per-item `estimatedHeight` shadows prop-level `estimatedRowHeight` (default 48). Smooth scroll: `scrollBehavior` prop drives auto-scroll-into-view + imperative API; per-call override supported. Sticky headers: items with `type: 'header'` render in body alongside rows; when `stickyHeaders={true}` the LAST header whose offset <= scrollTop pins to top via `position: sticky` + `translateY(scrollTop)`; sticky copy carries `data-sticky="true"`, body copy at that position omitted to avoid duplicates; offset math unaffected. Keyboard: ArrowDown/Up +/- 1; PageDown/Up +/- viewport/estimate items (min 1); Home -> 0; End -> last; active row auto-scrolls into view; disabled via `enableKeyboardNav={false}` (also flips root tabIndex to -1). End-reached: on every scroll computes `scrollHeight - scrollTop - clientHeight`; when <= `endReachedThreshold` (default 64 px) fires `onEndReached()`. ResizeObserver re-measures viewport on container resize (graceful fallback when unavailable). Pure helpers exported: `computeItemOffsets(items, measured, defaultHeight) -> offsets array (length items.length+1)`, `findVisibleRange(offsets, scrollTop, viewportHeight, overscan) -> {start, end}` (binary search by scrollTop + forward walk + overscan clamp), `findStickyHeaderIndex(items, offsets, scrollTop) -> index|null` (last header at or above scrollTop). ARIA: root `role="region"` + `tabIndex` (0 or -1 per enableKeyboardNav) + aria-label. Data attrs throughout (data-section + data-item-count + data-active-index + data-sticky-headers on root; data-section + data-item-id + data-item-index + data-item-type + data-active + data-disabled per row; data-section + data-sticky-index on sticky overlay; data-sticky=true on inner sticky item). forwardRef returns `ListVirtualizerHandle` imperative API. 42 new test cases in list-virtualizer.test.tsx (5 computeItemOffsets + 6 findVisibleRange + 4 findStickyHeaderIndex + 27 component); 42/42 pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented): horizontal virtualization (single column only), adaptive overscan from scroll velocity, anchored/pinned scroll on prepend (chat-window), row recycling pool (React reconciliation already covers), primitive-level onRowClick/onRowHover (host attaches via renderItem), role=list/listitem on every row (region role chosen since grouped rows + headers do not always map cleanly to a list). Keyboard: ArrowUp/Down increment/decrement focused field with wrap-around at bounds; step prop applies to minutes/seconds only (hours always by 1); ArrowUp/Down on AM/PM toggle flips period. Paste: onPaste on root passes clipboard text through pure helper parseTimeString(text, mode); accepts HH:MM, HH:MM:SS, HH.MM (dot separator), 'HH:MM AM/PM' (case-insensitive + a.m./p.m. dotted), 24-hour input in 12-mode auto-derives PM (15:30 -> 3:30 PM), 00:00 -> 12:00 AM; invalid pastes fall through to default. Wrap-around math via stepTimeField(current, delta, min, max) normalized through modulo across `range = max - min + 1` (e.g., stepTimeField(59, 5, 0, 59) -> 4 because 59+5=64; 64%60=4); 12-hour hour wrap (12->1 / 1->12); non-finite current -> min. Disabled/readOnly disable inputs + AM/PM toggle; data-disabled/data-read-only mirror on root. Controlled-or-uncontrolled via value/defaultValue + onChange. Pure helpers exported: normalizeTimeValue (mode-aware clamp + default period AM), stepTimeField (wrap-around increment), togglePeriod, parseTimeString (mode-aware parser; returns null on invalid), formatTimeValue (pad + colon + optional AM/PM suffix), to24HourFormat (12 AM -> 0; 12 PM -> 12; 3 PM -> 15), DEFAULT_TIME_VALUE_24 + DEFAULT_TIME_VALUE_12 constants. ARIA: root role=group + aria-label; inputs role=spinbutton + aria-valuemin/max/now/text + aria-label per field; separator aria-hidden=true; AM/PM toggle button aria-pressed + aria-label. Data attrs throughout (data-section + data-mode + data-show-seconds + data-disabled + data-read-only on root; data-section + data-time-field per input; data-section on separator; data-section + data-period on AM/PM toggle). forwardRef forwarded to root group div. 61 new test cases in time-picker.test.tsx (6 normalizeTimeValue + 6 stepTimeField + 2 togglePeriod + 10 parseTimeString + 3 formatTimeValue + 5 to24HourFormat + 29 component); 61/61 pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented): combined <DateTimePicker> (pair with DatePicker in host), time-zone selection (TimeValue is wall-clock; host owns zone), millisecond field (HH/MM/SS only for v1), range picker start+end time (separate composition), scroll-wheel mobile picker (native input + arrow keys canonical for v1), auto-advance to next field after two digits (adopter can layer via onChange + DOM ref). Reference /root/c4/arps-design-system-v1/. Branch c4/auto-ui-time-picker. Worker auto-w391. Bump 1.11.427. |

| 11.420 | UI: countdown-timer primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.438 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/countdown-timer.tsx` ships `<CountdownTimer>` -- counts down from a positive duration to zero, formats remaining time as `HH:MM:SS` (auto-collapses to `MM:SS` when the run never exceeds an hour), supports pause/resume/reset, and fires `onExpire` exactly once at zero. Optional warning + critical thresholds drive state-derived colour transitions and an ARIA live region tier swap. API: `durationSeconds`; `autoStart?` (default true); `warningThresholdSeconds?` (default 30) + `criticalThresholdSeconds?` (default 10); `controls?` (default true) + `showReset?` (default false); `format?: 'auto'|'hh:mm:ss'|'mm:ss'` (default 'auto'); event callbacks `onExpire`/`onTick(remaining)`/`onPause`/`onResume`/`onReset(seconds)`; `label?`; `ariaLabel?` (default 'Countdown timer'); `tickIntervalMs?` (default 250). Imperative `CountdownTimerHandle`: `start()` / `pause()` / `resume()` / `reset(seconds?)` / `toggle()` / `getRemainingSeconds()` / `getState()`. Tick loop computes remaining from a wall-clock `endsAt` timestamp so display stays accurate across throttled tabs and uneven `setInterval` cadence. Pause captures a snapshot + tears down the interval; resume re-derives `endsAt = now + snapshot` so accumulated drift never leaks. `onExpire` fires exactly once at zero (guarded by a ref so React strict-mode double renders do not duplicate). State derivation: `<= 0` -> 'expired', `<= critical` -> 'critical', `<= warning` -> 'warning', otherwise 'normal'. Display text class swaps with state (`text-foreground` / `text-warning` / `text-destructive`); ARIA `aria-live` flips to 'assertive' when state is 'critical' so SRs announce the imminent expiration. Toggle button auto-disables when remaining=0 (no resume from expired without reset). Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_WARNING_THRESHOLD=30` / `DEFAULT_CRITICAL_THRESHOLD=10` / `DEFAULT_COUNTDOWN_FORMAT='auto'` / `DEFAULT_TICK_INTERVAL_MS=250`; `clampCountdownDuration(value)` floors negatives + `+Infinity` to 0; `formatCountdownTime(seconds, format?, thresholdHours?)` ceils fractional seconds (0.5s -> '00:01'), 'auto' includes hours only at 1h+, 'mm:ss' collapses ('62:05' for 1h2m5s); `getCountdownState(remaining, warning?, critical?)` returns 'expired' for 0/neg/NaN; `tickRemaining(remaining, deltaMs)` subtracts deltaMs/1000 and clamps to 0. ARIA: region `role="region"` + aria-label; display `role="timer"` + `aria-atomic="true"` + `aria-live` polite (or assertive in critical); toggle `aria-label="Pause countdown"|"Resume countdown"`; reset `aria-label="Reset countdown"`. Data attrs throughout (data-section per node: `countdown-timer` / `-label` / `-display` / `-controls` / `-toggle` / `-reset`; root mirrors live state via `data-state` / `data-running` / `data-format` / `data-remaining`). 48 new test cases in countdown-timer.test.tsx (5 clampCountdownDuration + 6 formatCountdownTime + 5 getCountdownState + 2 tickRemaining + 4 constants + 23 component synchronous + 3 fake-timer driven); 48/48 pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. | 11.422 | UI: scroll-spy primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.440 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/scroll-spy.tsx` ships `<ScrollSpy>` -- a `<nav>` whose active item tracks the section currently in the viewport. `IntersectionObserver` watches every linked section; clicking an item smooth-scrolls the target into view with an optional offset for sticky headers. API: `items: ScrollSpyItem[]` (id/label/disabled?); `activeId?` (controlled) / `defaultActiveId?` (uncontrolled seed) + `onActiveChange(id)`; `rootMargin?` (default '0px 0px -50% 0px') + `threshold?` (default 0); `scrollBehavior?: 'smooth'|'auto'` (default 'smooth'); `orientation?: 'vertical'|'horizontal'` (default 'vertical'); `ariaLabel?` (default 'Section navigation'); `scrollOffset?` (px, default 0); `renderItem?` render-prop replaces the default link. Items render as a `<ul>` of links by default; each link is `aria-current="location"` while matching the active id. `renderItem` swaps the default link for any host-rendered element while keeping the per-item `<li>` wrapper with its `data-section` markers. On click the matching section is found by id and scrolled into view: `scrollOffset=0` uses `element.scrollIntoView({ behavior, block: 'start' })`; otherwise `scrollIntoViewWithOffset` falls back to `window.scrollTo({ top: rect.top + scrollY - offset, behavior })` so sticky-header layouts can park the section below the header. `IntersectionObserver` observes only items whose matching `document.getElementById` exists; default `rootMargin '0px 0px -50% 0px'` treats the upper half of the viewport as the "active band" so the active id flips when the section reaches the middle line. When no entries intersect the active id is preserved unless the previously-active section is itself in the current batch (means it just scrolled out -> clear). Controlled `activeId` always wins for the rendered highlight; observer still emits `onActiveChange` so the host can use the callback for analytics/routing while keeping a one-way data flow. Observer disconnects on unmount and on every prop change that resets the watch list. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_SCROLL_SPY_ROOT_MARGIN` / `DEFAULT_SCROLL_SPY_THRESHOLD=0` / `DEFAULT_SCROLL_SPY_ORIENTATION='vertical'` / `DEFAULT_SCROLL_SPY_OFFSET=0`; `ScrollSpyEntry` interface (minimal shape consumed by helpers so adopters can unit-test their own observers without instantiating real DOM entries); `getMostVisibleEntry(entries)` picks the entry with the highest intersectionRatio that is also isIntersecting; `getActiveIdFromEntries(entries, previousActive)` -- consults getMostVisibleEntry first, when nothing intersects preserves previous (unless previous is in the batch, indicating it just left); `scrollIntoViewWithOffset(element, offset?, behavior?)` -- jsdom-safe, falls back to `element.scrollIntoView` when window.scrollTo is missing. ARIA: root `<nav>` + aria-label; default link `aria-current="location"` when active + `aria-disabled` when item.disabled. Data attrs throughout (data-section per node: `scroll-spy` / `-list` / `-item` / `-link`; each LI mirrors `data-item-id` / `data-active` / `data-disabled`; root mirrors `data-orientation` / `data-active-id` / `data-item-count`). forwardRef forwarded to the `<nav>`. 41 new test cases in scroll-spy.test.tsx (2 getMostVisibleEntry + 3 getActiveIdFromEntries + 3 scrollIntoViewWithOffset + 4 constants + 29 component); test file ships a `MockIntersectionObserver` class wired via window assignment with an `emit(entries)` test helper for deterministic viewport simulation; 41/41 pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented): scroll-restoration (host owns hash routing), nested/hierarchical spying (host composes multiple ScrollSpy instances), configurable observer `root` (always documentElement for v1), bidirectional auto-scroll (the spy follows scroll position; does not reverse-drive scroll from the rendered list). Reference /root/c4/arps-design-system-v1/. Branch c4/auto-ui-scroll-spy. Worker auto-w404. Bump 1.11.440. |
| 11.423 | UI: back-to-top primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.441 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/back-to-top.tsx` ships `<BackToTop>` -- a floating action button that appears once the page (or a custom scroll container) has been scrolled past a configurable threshold and smooth-scrolls the watched target back to its top on click. API: `threshold?` (px, default 200); `scrollBehavior?: 'smooth'|'auto'` (default 'smooth'); `scrollTarget?: HTMLElement|Window|null` (default window); `ariaLabel?` (default 'Back to top'); `position?: 'bottom-right'|'bottom-left'|'bottom-center'` (default 'bottom-right'); `icon?` (default ArrowUp from lucide); `showLabel?` (default false) + `label?` (default 'Back to top'); `onClick?`; `initiallyVisible?` (SSR / test override; default false); `visible?` (fully controlled); `hideOnVisible?` (default true). Renders a `<button>` fixed to one of three corner positions with opacity-based fade transition. Subscribes to the watched target's scroll event with `{ passive: true }`; listener detaches on unmount. Initial visibility is computed from `initiallyVisible` and then upgraded to true on mount **only when the current scroll position already meets the threshold** -- preserves an explicit `initiallyVisible=true` override on fresh page (scrollY=0) while still revealing the button when the user navigates to a deep-link/restored scroll position past the threshold. Click handler fires `onClick`, calls `scrollTargetToTop(target, scrollBehavior)`, and (when uncontrolled + `hideOnVisible`) optimistically hides the button; next scroll event re-syncs once smooth-scroll lands at zero. Controlled `visible` always wins (clicks still call scroll target + onClick but do not flip local state). Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_BACK_TO_TOP_THRESHOLD=200` / `DEFAULT_BACK_TO_TOP_POSITION='bottom-right'` / `DEFAULT_BACK_TO_TOP_LABEL='Back to top'`; `shouldShowBackToTop(scrollY, threshold?)` -- inclusive at threshold (200px scroll with 200px threshold counts as "show"), negative thresholds collapse to 0, NaN inputs return false; `getScrollTop(target)` -- accepts window / HTMLElement / null, reads scrollY for window and scrollTop for elements, falls back to document.documentElement.scrollTop when window.scrollY is missing; `scrollTargetToTop(target, behavior?)` -- uses window.scrollTo / element.scrollTo, falls back to setting `element.scrollTop = 0` when scrollTo is missing (jsdom-safe). ARIA: button `aria-label` (default 'Back to top'); `aria-hidden="true"` when invisible (removed from accessibility tree until needed); `tabIndex=-1` when hidden, `0` when visible. Data attrs throughout (data-section per node: `back-to-top` / `-icon` / `-label`; button mirrors `data-visible` ('true'/'false') + `data-position`). forwardRef forwarded to the button. 46 new test cases in back-to-top.test.tsx (7 shouldShowBackToTop + 4 getScrollTop + 4 scrollTargetToTop + 3 constants + 28 component); 46/46 pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Dismissal is persisted to `localStorage` under a per-tour id so users do not see the same tour twice. API: `tourId` (localStorage namespace); `steps: FeatureTourStep[]` (id/target/title/description?/placement?); `open?` (controlled) + `defaultOpen?` (default true; honours persisted dismissal) + `onOpenChange`; `stepIndex?` (controlled) + `defaultStepIndex?` (default 0) + `onStepChange(index)`; `onComplete` / `onSkip`; `storageKey?` overrides the namespaced key; `showMask?` (default true); `closeOnEscape?` (default true); `showProgress?` (default true); `panelOffset?` (default 12); `labels?: { prev?, next?, skip?, finish?, closeAria? }`; `containerId?` (portal root id, default 'app-portal-root'); `ariaLabel?` (default 'Feature tour'). Spotlight ring is drawn around the current anchor's bounding rect. Tooltip panel sits next to the anchor using `computeTourPanelPosition` (placement defaults to 'bottom'; 'auto' uses exported `resolveAutoPlacement` heuristic: bottom > top > right > left). Anchor + panel position re-measured on resize and capture-phase scroll. If selector misses, panel falls back to viewport centre + spotlight omitted + root carries `data-anchor-found="false"`. Controls: Prev disabled on first step; Next advances and becomes Finish on last step -> fires onComplete + persists dismissal + closes; Skip fires onSkip + persists dismissal + closes; X close button closes manually (no dismissal). Keyboard: Escape -> Skip (when closeOnEscape); ArrowRight -> Next; ArrowLeft -> Prev. `defaultOpen` honours persisted dismissal flag (second mount with same tourId stays closed); controlled `open` bypasses the flag for "Replay tour". Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_FEATURE_TOUR_STORAGE_PREFIX='c4:feature-tour:'` / `DEFAULT_FEATURE_TOUR_PLACEMENT='bottom'` / `DEFAULT_FEATURE_TOUR_PANEL_WIDTH=320` / `DEFAULT_FEATURE_TOUR_PANEL_OFFSET=12`; `getTourStorageKey(tourId, override?)`; `isTourDismissed` / `markTourDismissed` / `clearTourDismissal` -- swallow throws from private-mode/quota/null storage so the primitive never crashes the host; `clampStepIndex(index, total)` -- empty total -> 0, NaN -> 0, clamps to `[0, total-1]`; `resolveAutoPlacement(anchor, panel, viewport, offset?)` -- bottom > top > right > left heuristic; `computeTourPanelPosition(anchor, panel, placement?, viewport?, offset?)` -- placement math + viewport clamping so panel never scrolls off-screen. ARIA: panel `role="dialog"` + `aria-modal="true"` + aria-label + `aria-labelledby` pointing to step title id; close button `aria-label="Close tour"` (customisable). Data attrs throughout (data-section per node: `feature-tour` / `-mask` / `-spotlight` / `-panel` / `-header` / `-title` / `-description` / `-progress` / `-actions` / `-skip` / `-prev` / `-next` / `-close`; root mirrors `data-tour-id` / `data-step-index` / `data-step-id` / `data-step-count` / `data-anchor-found` / `data-placement`). 55 new test cases in feature-tour.test.tsx (2 getTourStorageKey + 6 dismissal round-trip + 6 clampStepIndex + 4 resolveAutoPlacement + 6 computeTourPanelPosition + 3 constants + 28 component); 55/55 pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented): multi-target highlighting per step (single anchor per step), branching/conditional steps based on user input (host drives stepIndex), animated panel transitions on step change (snap for v1), server-side configuration of tour content (host owns steps prop; persistent dismissal is the only state the primitive owns). Each entry rendered with a level chip, time stamp, optional component/source tag, and a message body that is ANSI-color-parsed + search-highlighted. API: `entries: LogEntry[]` (id/timestamp/level/message/component?/source?); `levels?` (default all 6); `enabledLevels?` (controlled) + `defaultEnabledLevels?` + `onEnabledLevelsChange`; `query?` (controlled) + `defaultQuery?` + `onQueryChange`; `isPaused?` (controlled) + `defaultPaused?` + `onPausedChange`; `timeRange?` (controlled) + `defaultTimeRange?` + `onTimeRangeChange`; `autoScroll?` (default true); `maxHeight?` (default 320); `ariaLabel?` (default 'Log stream'); `emptyState?` (default 'No log entries'); `showSearch?` / `showTimeRange?` / `showClear?` (default true/true/false); `onClear?`. The list scroll container auto-scrolls to bottom whenever the filtered entry count changes -- unless `isPaused` is true. We track lastLengthRef so adopters that re-render the array don't retrigger scroll on no-op rerender. Level chips are `role="switch"` + `aria-checked`; clicking toggles in the enabled set + fires onChange with the ordered subset (canonical = LOG_LEVELS). Search input filters on message + component + source (case-insensitive substring); matches wrapped in `<mark>` via highlightLogMatches. Time-range start + end are `<input type="datetime-local">` fields; clearing a field deletes the corresponding key. Pause button swaps aria-label between "Pause stream" / "Resume stream" + Pause/Play icons. Clear button opt-in via showClear + onClear. Pure helpers exported: `LOG_LEVELS = ['trace','debug','info','warn','error','fatal']`; `getLogLevelRank` / `getLogLevelClass`; `formatLogTimestamp(value)` -- HH:MM:SS.cs, empty for falsy/unparseable, accepts Date/number/string; `inLogTimeRange(ts, range?)` -- undefined / start / end / both bounds; `filterLogEntries(entries, { enabledLevels?, query?, timeRange? })` -- combines all three; `parseAnsi(input): AnsiSegment[]` -- consumes 30..37 / 40..47 / 90..97 / 100..107 (fg/bg standard + bright), 1/2/3/4 (bold/dim/italic/underline), 22/23/24 (resets), 39/49 (fg/bg resets), 0 / bare ESC[m (full reset); unknown codes are no-ops so parser never throws; `highlightLogMatches(text, query?)` -- regex-special-escaped, case-insensitive. ARIA: region root + aria-label; level toggle role=switch + aria-checked; search aria-label="Filter log entries"; time range inputs aria-label; pause aria-label swaps; clear aria-label. Data attrs throughout (data-section per node: `log-stream` / `-controls` / `-level-filter` / `-level-toggle` / `-search` / `-search-input` / `-time-range` / `-time-range-start-label` / `-time-range-start` / `-time-range-end-label` / `-time-range-end` / `-pause` / `-clear` / `-list` / `-empty` / `-entries` / `-entry` / `-entry-time` / `-entry-level` / `-entry-component` / `-entry-message` / `-entry-segment` / `-entry-source` / `-mark`; root mirrors data-paused / -entry-count / -filtered-count / -auto-scroll; level toggle mirrors data-level / -enabled; entry mirrors data-entry-id / -level). forwardRef forwarded to the list scroll container. 54 new test cases in log-stream.test.tsx (1 LOG_LEVELS + 1 getLogLevelRank + 1 getLogLevelClass + 3 formatLogTimestamp + 4 inLogTimeRange + 5 filterLogEntries + 8 parseAnsi + 3 highlightLogMatches + 28 component); 54/54 pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented): server-side log subscription (host owns fetch/SSE/WebSocket and passes entries), virtualisation for very long streams (host wraps in `<VirtualizedList>` past a few thousand entries), color-256 / truecolor ANSI parsing (only standard 16-color palette; truecolor sequences parse as resets), persisting filter state across reloads (host owns persistence via controlled props). Hovering a slice expands it outward by a small offset, a legend lists every slice with its color + percentage, optional per-slice percent labels sit on top of the arc, and the donut variant renders a configurable total readout in the centre. The root carries an `aria-describedby` reference to a visually-hidden text region that summarises every slice for screen readers. API: `data: readonly ChartPieSlice[]` (id/label/value/color?); `width?` (default 320) + `height?` (default 240); `innerRadius?` (>0 -> donut) + `outerRadius?` (auto-fit when omitted); `showLegend?` (default true) + `showPercentLabels?` (default false) + `showTotal?` (default true); `totalLabel?`; `formatValue?` + `formatPercent?`; `animate?` (default true); `ariaLabel?` (default 'Pie chart') + `ariaDescription?`; `onSliceClick(slice)`; `startAngle?` (radians; default -PI/2); `hoverExpand?` (default 6 px); `legendPlacement?: 'right'|'bottom'`; `legendFormat?`; `emptyState?` (default 'No data'). Computes percent + arc range per slice from a positive total; non-positive / NaN values dropped before layout. Slices start at `startAngle` and sweep clockwise. Hover expands the active slice by `hoverExpand` (recomputes arc with larger outer radius); mouse-leave/blur collapses. Donut mode kicks in when `innerRadius>0`: pie wedge `M/L/A/Z`; donut annular segment `M/A/L/A/Z`. Donut centre readout: total formatted via `formatValue` sits at geometric centre with optional `totalLabel` below. Legend renders one row per slice with color swatch + label + percent; `legendFormat` overrides the body. ARIA description rendered as `sr-only <p>` alongside the SVG; `ariaDescription` override replaces default comma-joined summary. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_PIE_WIDTH=320` / `DEFAULT_CHART_PIE_HEIGHT=240` / `DEFAULT_CHART_PIE_HOVER_EXPAND=6`; `getPieTotal(data)` -- sums positive finite values (NaN/Infinity/negatives dropped); `computePieSlices(data, startAngle?)` -- returns ComputedSlice per entry with startAngle/endAngle/midAngle/percent/value; empty/zero-total -> empty array; `polarToCartesian(cx, cy, r, angle)`; `arcPath(cx, cy, innerR, outerR, startAngle, endAngle)` -- handles pie wedges + annular segments + full-circle/annulus split into two semicircles; `formatPiePercent(percent, formatter?)` -- one decimal under 10%, zero decimals at/above 10%, 100% at >= 99.95. ARIA: region root + aria-label + aria-describedby; svg role=img + aria-label; per-slice group `role="graphics-symbol"` + `aria-label="<label>: <percent>"` + tabIndex=0. Data attrs throughout (data-section per node: `chart-pie` / `-canvas` / `-svg` / `-aria-desc` / `-empty` / `-slice` / `-arc` / `-label` / `-center` / `-center-total` / `-center-label` / `-legend` / `-legend-item` / `-legend-swatch` / `-legend-label` / `-legend-percent`; root mirrors `data-slice-count` / `data-donut` / `data-animate`; slices mirror `data-slice-id` + `data-hovered`; legend rows mirror `data-slice-id`; legend wrapper mirrors `data-placement`). forwardRef forwarded to root region. 53 new test cases in chart-pie.test.tsx (3 getPieTotal + 6 computePieSlices + 2 polarToCartesian + 4 arcPath + 5 formatPiePercent + 1 constants + 32 component); 53/53 pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented): nested/sunburst hierarchies (host wraps multi-ring layer), slice connector lines for outside labels (host adds custom SVG children), 3D shading (intentionally flat vector for accessibility + legibility), animated slice rotation beyond mount fade (host wraps in motion primitive). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-area.tsx` ships `<ChartArea>` -- pure-SVG area chart with multi-series support, an `overlaid` (each series fills from baseline 0) and `stacked` (cumulative-sum baseline) mode toggle, hover tooltip listing every series at the cursor, axis grid + optional tick labels, and a smooth-curve toggle. API: `series: ChartAreaSeries[]` (id/label/data/color?); each data point has `{x, y}`; `mode?: 'overlaid'|'stacked'` (default 'overlaid'); `width?` (default 520) + `height?` (default 280) + `padding?` (default 36); `axisLabel?: { x?, y? }`; `smooth?` (default false); `showGrid?` / `showTooltip?` / `showAxisTicks?` / `showLines?` / `animate?` (all default true); `fillOpacity?` (default 0.35); `formatX?` + `formatY?`; `tickCount?` (default 4); `xDomain?` / `yDomain?`. `buildAreaStack` reshapes the input series for the configured mode: overlaid -> y0=0+y1=value per point; stacked -> cumulative baseline tracked per-x (each series stacks on top of the previous, negatives clamp to 0 so cumulative sums never regress). Bottom edge always traces back along per-point baseline (y0). `showLines=true` (default) draws top edge as a separate stroke path; showLines=false removes the stroke. New `web/src/components/ui/chart-heatmap.tsx` ships `<ChartHeatmap>` -- calendar-style heatmap (GitHub-contributions layout). Each column is an ISO week; each row is a day-of-week starting at the configured `weekStartsOn`. Cells are coloured along a 5-step quantile scale (no-data / q1 / q2 / q3 / q4) so adopters can read intensity at a glance. All date math runs in UTC so cells never drift across DST / timezones. Drop-off labels between consecutive stages quantify users lost; hover opens a tooltip with stage label + formatted value + % of top stage + % conversion from previous (omitted on the first stage). Default colour gradient flows from '#bfdbfe' at the top to '#1d4ed8' at the bottom; per-stage colour and gradient endpoints both overridable. API: `stages: ChartFunnelStage[]` ({id, label, value, color?}); `width?` (default 360) / `height?` (default 320) / `stageGap?` (default 4); `showDropoff?` / `showValues?` / `showLabels?` / `showTooltip?` / `animate?` (all default true); `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Funnel chart') / `ariaDescription?`; `formatValue?` / `formatPercent?`; `onStageClick({stage, index, dropoff, conversion, ofTop})`; `gradient?: {from?, to?}`. Geometry: each stage's slice width is `(width - 16) * value / max` at its top; bottom continues into the next stage's top width; final stage tapers to half its top width by default so the visual still funnels. Mount animation motion-safe:animate-fade-in per stage group. ARIA description auto-summary: 'Funnel with N stages. <stage> <value> (<ofTop%> of top). ...'; empty -> 'No data'. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_FUNNEL_WIDTH/HEIGHT/STAGE_GAP/GRADIENT_FROM/GRADIENT_TO`; `getFunnelMax(stages)` -- max of values; fallback 1; `getFunnelRatio(value, max)` -- clamps to [0,1]; non-finite/non-positive/zero-max -> 0; `getStageDropoff(prev, curr)` -- prev - curr when positive; first stage / non-finite / over-prev / non-positive guards -> 0; `getStageConversion(prev, curr)` -- curr/prev in [0,1]; first stage -> 1; non-positive guards -> 0; `getStageOfTop(top, value)` -- value/top in [0,1]; non-positive/non-finite -> 0; over-top clamps to 1; `interpolateColor(from, to, t)` -- hex (incl #rgb shorthand) lerp; parse failure -> from; t clamped to [0,1]; `buildFunnelPath(topW, bottomW, top, height, cx)` -- closed quadrilateral SVG path; negative widths clamp to zero; `describeFunnelChart(stages, formatValue?, formatPercent?)` -- ARIA summary. ARIA: region root + role=img svg + sr-only auto-description span; per-slice role=graphics-symbol + tabIndex 0 (focus opens tooltip via onFocus); tooltip role=tooltip. Data attrs throughout (chart-funnel / -aria-desc / -svg / -stage / -slice / -label / -value / -dropoff / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-value / -tooltip-of-top / -tooltip-conversion; root mirrors data-stage-count / -animate; stage groups mirror data-stage-id / -stage-index / -stage-color / -hovered; drop-off text mirrors data-dropoff / -conversion). 60 vitest cases (2 getFunnelMax + 3 getFunnelRatio + 5 getStageDropoff + 4 getStageConversion + 4 getStageOfTop + 6 interpolateColor + 2 buildFunnelPath + 3 describeFunnelChart + 1 constants + 30 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. New `web/src/components/ui/chart-treemap.tsx` ships `<ChartTreemap>` -- pure-SVG hierarchical treemap with a squarified layout (Bruls / Huijsen / van Wijk 1999). Click-to-drill descends into the hovered node; the drill path is fully controllable and emits `onDrillChange` so adopters can wire breadcrumbs or back buttons. Drill semantics: clicking a parent pushes its id onto the path; leaf clicks do not drill. | 11.454 | UI: chart-network primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.472 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-network.tsx` ships `<ChartNetwork>` -- pure-SVG force-directed network graph. Nodes are placed by a deterministic physics simulation (Coulomb repulsion + edge spring + center gravity) that runs `iterations` steps on mount or data change. Edges paint as thin lines between nodes with thickness scaling to edge weight. Drag a node to reposition; pinned nodes stay put while the layout re-runs around them. Mouse-wheel zooms; drag the background to pan. Built-in zoom controls (+, -, 1:1) in the top-right corner. Hover opens a tooltip with node label + degree + optional group; per-node and per-edge click callbacks fire with full payloads. API: `nodes: ChartNetworkNode[]` ({id, label, group?, weight?, color?, x?, y?, fixed?}) + `edges: ChartNetworkEdge[]` ({source, target, weight?, label?, color?}); `width?` (default 600) / `height?` (default 400); `iterations?` (default 80); `repulsion?` (800) / `springLength?` (50) / `springStrength?` (0.05) / `gravity?` (0.005) / `damping?` (0.85); `defaultNodeRadius?` (8) / `defaultNodeColor?` ('#2563eb') / `defaultEdgeColor?` ('#94a3b8'); `showLabels?` / `showTooltip?` / `showZoomControls?` / `enableDrag?` / `enableZoom?` / `enablePan?` / `animate?` (all default true); `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Network graph') / `ariaDescription?`; `formatValue?`; `onNodeClick({node, degree})` + `onEdgeClick({edge, source, target})`. Initial layout: nodes with explicit (x,y) keep position; others land on a golden-angle spiral centered on canvas. Simulation guards against NaN by jittering identical positions. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_NETWORK_WIDTH/HEIGHT/ITERATIONS/REPULSION/SPRING_LENGTH/SPRING_STRENGTH/GRAVITY/DAMPING/NODE_RADIUS/NODE_COLOR/EDGE_COLOR`; `seedNetworkPositions(nodes, width, height)` -- deterministic golden-angle spiral seed; preserves explicit coords + fixed flag; `stepForceSimulation(nodes, edges, params)` -- pure single step; pinned stationary; no input mutation; NaN-jitter guard; `runForceLayout(nodes, edges, params, iterations)` -- full deterministic layout; iter=0 returns seed; `getNetworkBounds(nodes)` -- min/max; empty/non-finite fallback {0,0,1,1}; `computeNodeDegree(nodeId, edges)` -- incident-edge count; isolated -> 0; `findNodeAtPoint(nodes, x, y, radius)` -- closest within radius or null; centermost at radius=0; `getNodeRadius(node, defaultRadius)` -- sqrt(weight) scaling; floor 2; fallback for missing/invalid weight; `describeNetworkChart(nodes, edges, formatValue?)` -- top-5 by degree summary. New `web/src/components/ui/chart-mosaic.tsx` ships `<ChartMosaic>` -- pure-SVG mosaic plot for 2D contingency tables. Each column's width is proportional to its marginal total; within each column, row cells stack with heights proportional to the conditional counts. Cell fill encodes the standardized chi-square residual `(O - E) / sqrt(E)` -- blue ('#1d4ed8') for positive (more than expected), red ('#b91c1c') for negative (less than expected), neutral ('#f1f5f9') for zero; configurable `residualClamp` (default 3) caps colour saturation. | 11.461 | UI: chart-parallel primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.479 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-parallel.tsx` ships `<ChartParallel>` -- pure-SVG parallel coordinates plot. Each dimension becomes a vertical axis; each row becomes a polyline crossing every axis at the value for that dimension. Drag on an axis (within its 16-px hit-rect) to brush a y-range -- rows whose values fall within every active brush stay visible; the rest fade to 0.08 opacity but still render. Hovering a row highlights it and dims the others. Double-click an axis to clear its brush. Brushes are fully controllable via `brushes` + `onBrushesChange` for host-driven filter state; `defaultBrushes` for uncontrolled initial state. Rows missing a dimension value snap to that axis's centre so the polyline stays continuous. Brushes AND-combine; rows with non-finite values for any brushed dimension fail the check. New `web/src/components/ui/chart-arc-diagram.tsx` ships `<ChartArcDiagram>` -- pure-SVG arc diagram. Nodes sit on a horizontal baseline, each rendered as a dot whose radius can be scaled by `node.weight`. New `web/src/components/ui/chart-radar-spider.tsx` ships `<ChartRadarSpider>` -- pure-SVG spider/radar variant distinct from `<ChartRadar>` (11.445). Where ChartRadar renders one filled polygon per series (colour-by-series), ChartRadarSpider decomposes each series's polygon into per-axis wedges: each wedge is the triangle from chart centre through the data point at axis N to the data point at axis N+1, coloured by axis. | 11.469 | UI: chart-donut primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.487 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-donut.tsx` ships `<ChartDonut>` -- pure-SVG donut chart (pie variant with a center hole). Each slice paints an annular arc; the hollow center hosts a configurable two-line label group (primary value + smaller secondary line). Distinct from `<ChartPie>` (11.440) in that this primitive introduces a first-class center slot with a default visible-total readout, a configurable `thicknessRatio` (clamped to [0, 1]; default 0.32) that drives the inner radius (= `outerRadius * (1 - thicknessRatio)`), optional `padAngle` (default 0.012 rad) deducted between consecutive arcs (only when more than one slice is visible), and optional `cornerRadius` for rounded arc ends. Default `startAngle = -pi/2` so the first slice begins at 12 o'clock. Hover/focus on an arc sets the hovered id and opens a tooltip with label, formatted value, and formatted percent; `onArcClick({slice, arc})` fires on click. Legend interaction: every entry is a focusable `<button aria-pressed>` per slice; controlled (`hiddenSlices` + `onHiddenSlicesChange`) and uncontrolled (`defaultHiddenSlices`). Hidden slices reproportion the visible ring; `onSliceToggle({slice, hidden})` fires with the next state. Center slot resolution: primary = `centerValue` > `centerContent.primary` > formatted visible total (suppressed via `showCenterTotal=false`); secondary = `centerLabel` > `centerContent.secondary`; if neither line resolves the group is omitted. `showCenter=false` removes the group entirely. Optional in-arc labels (`showLabels=true`) paint the formatted percent at the arc midpoint for slices whose fraction exceeds 5%. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per arc (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `slices: readonly ChartDonutSlice[]` ({id, label, value, color?}) / `width?` (320) / `height?` (320) / `padding?` (24) / `thicknessRatio?` (0.32) / `padAngle?` (0.012) / `cornerRadius?` (0) / `startAngle?` (-pi/2) / `hiddenSlices?` / `defaultHiddenSlices?` / `onHiddenSlicesChange?` / `showLegend?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `showCenter?` (true) / `showLabels?` (false) / `showCenterTotal?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `centerContent?` / `centerLabel?` / `centerValue?` / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Donut chart') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatPercent?` / `legendPlacement?` ('right'\|'bottom', default 'bottom') / `onArcClick?({slice, arc})` / `onSliceToggle?({slice, hidden})` / `style?`. | 11.470 | UI: chart-bubble primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.488 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-bubble.tsx` ships `<ChartBubble>` -- pure-SVG bubble chart encoding three numeric dimensions per datum: `x` (x-axis position), `y` (y-axis position), and `size` (drives bubble radius via sqrt-area scaling between `minRadius`/`maxRadius`). Optional per-point `category` drives palette-based color encoding (`getBubbleCategoryColor` maps category -> palette index via first-seen order across the data); per-point `color` override beats the palette. Distinct from `<ChartScatter>` (11.444) in that bubbles have a 3rd encoded variable (size) instead of uniform dot radius, and distinct from `<ChartDotPlot>` (11.465) in that the x axis is numeric here rather than categorical. Layout: `computeBubbleLayout` drops non-finite-x / non-finite-y entries, skips hidden category/id, then projects `(x, y)` into the inner canvas with SVG-y-down convention (yMax at top, yMin at bottom). Bounds: auto-derived via `getBubbleBounds`; collapsed x/y range expands by +/-0.5; non-finite x/y ignored; controlled via `xMin`/`xMax`/`yMin`/`yMax` props. Size encoding: sqrt-area interpolation; collapsed size range falls back to `(min+max)/2`; non-finite/negative -> 0 -> `minRadius`. Hover/focus on a bubble sets the hovered id and opens a tooltip with label, category (when present), x, y, size (each formatted). Legend (rendered only when at least one point has a category): focusable `<button aria-pressed>` per category; controlled (`hiddenCategories` + `onHiddenCategoriesChange`) and uncontrolled (`defaultHiddenCategories`); `onCategoryToggle({category, hidden})` fires on click. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per bubble (suppressed via `animate=false`). Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_BUBBLE_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/TICK_COUNT/MIN_RADIUS/MAX_RADIUS/COLOR/PALETTE`; `getBubbleDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; non-finite/negative -> color 0; `getBubbleBounds(points)` -- min/max for x/y/size; empty -> (0..1, 0..1, 0..0); collapsed expansion; non-finite skipped; `getBubbleRadius(size, sizeMin, sizeMax, minR, maxR)` -- sqrt-area interpolation; collapsed range -> (min+max)/2; `getBubbleCategories(points)` -- unique non-empty in first-seen order; `getBubbleCategoryColor(category, categories)` -- palette lookup; unknown/null -> default color; `getBubbleTicks(min, max, count?)` -- evenly-spaced; collapsed -> [min]; `computeBubbleLayout({points, hidden, categories, bounds, innerW, innerH, padX, padY, minRadius, maxRadius})` -- canonical layout returning `{ id, label, category, color, cx, cy, r, x, y, size, index }[]`; `describeBubbleChart(points, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Bubble chart with N bubbles[ across M categories]. x range <xMin> to <xMax>; y range <yMin> to <yMax>."; empty / all-invalid -> "No data". | 11.471 | UI: chart-calendar-heatmap primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.489 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-calendar-heatmap.tsx` ships `<ChartCalendarHeatmap>` -- pure-SVG GitHub-style year calendar heatmap. Each day paints as a small rounded square; columns are weeks; rows are days of the week. Color encodes intensity via a configurable 5-step palette plus a distinct emptyColor for zero / non-positive / non-finite days. Month labels render above the grid at the first column that touches each new month (one label per month visible in the requested range); a sparse DOW label axis renders on the left (3 labels by default, weekStart-aware). Distinct from `<ChartHeatmap>` (11.442) in that this primitive is *time-aware*: it knows about ISO dates, week boundaries, and months -- callers hand it `[{date, value}]` and either a `year` prop (default = current UTC year) or explicit `startDate` / `endDate`, and get the full layout for free. Range resolution: when both `startDate` + `endDate` are present they are used verbatim; otherwise `year` (or the current UTC year) materialises Jan 1 -> Dec 31 via `getYearRange`. Layout: `computeCalendarHeatmap` pads the start of the grid back to the previous `weekStart` boundary so every day falls on the correct row; days outside the requested range (the pre-pad days in the first column) are not emitted. Color: zero / non-finite / negative values paint with `emptyColor` (level 0); non-zero values map via `ceil(ratio * paletteLength)` so the smallest positive value still gets palette[0] rather than the empty color; ratios over 1 clamp to the top step. Hover/focus on a cell opens a tooltip with formatted date + value; per-cell click handler. ARIA / keyboard: every cell is `role="graphics-symbol"` + `tabIndex={0}` so the whole year is keyboard-tabbable. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per cell (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `values: readonly ChartCalendarHeatmapValue[]` ({date: string YYYY-MM-DD, value: number}) / `startDate?` / `endDate?` / `year?` / `weekStart?` (0=Sun, 1=Mon; default 0) / `cellSize?` (12) / `cellGap?` (3) / `topPad?` (18) / `leftPad?` (28) / `rightPad?` (8) / `bottomPad?` (22) / `palette?` (5-step green) / `emptyColor?` ('#e5e7eb') / `maxValue?` / `showMonthLabels?` (true) / `showDowLabels?` (true) / `showLegend?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `monthLabels?` / `dowLabels?` / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Calendar heatmap') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatDate?` / `onCellClick?(cell)` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_CALENDAR_HEATMAP_CELL_SIZE/CELL_GAP/TOP_PAD/LEFT_PAD/RIGHT_PAD/BOTTOM_PAD/EMPTY_COLOR/PALETTE/MONTH_LABELS/DOW_LABELS`; `toISODate(d)` / `parseISODate(s)` -- UTC formatting + parsing, rejects malformed + impossible dates (e.g. 2024-02-30); `addDays(d, n)` -- month + year crossing; `getYearRange(year)` -- Jan 1 -> Dec 31 UTC; `getCalendarHeatmapColor(value, max, palette?, emptyColor?)` -- returns {color, level}; level 0 = empty; 1..palette.length = palette step; `computeCalendarHeatmap(input)` -- canonical layout returning `{ weeks, cells, monthLabels, width, height, max, weekStart, cellSize, cellGap, topPad, leftPad }`; invalid / inverted range -> empty result; `describeCalendarHeatmap(values, start, end, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Calendar heatmap from <start> to <end>. N active days, total <sum>, peak <peak>."; invalid range -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-calendar-heatmap-aria-desc"` span; per-cell `<rect role="graphics-symbol" tabIndex={0}>` with aria-label `"<formatted date>: <formatted value>"`. data-section on every node (chart-calendar-heatmap / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -months / -month-label / -dow / -dow-label / -cells / -cell / -tooltip / -tooltip-date / -tooltip-value / -legend / -legend-low / -legend-high / -legend-swatch); root mirrors data-cell-count, data-week-count, data-week-start, data-start-date, data-end-date, data-max, data-animate; cells mirror data-cell-date, data-cell-value, data-cell-level, data-cell-color, data-cell-col, data-cell-row, data-hovered; month labels mirror data-month-index, data-month-col; DOW labels mirror data-dow-row; legend swatches mirror data-legend-level. 52 vitest cases (1 constants + 3 toISODate/parseISODate + 2 addDays + 1 getYearRange + 5 getCalendarHeatmapColor + 12 computeCalendarHeatmap + 3 describeCalendarHeatmap + 25 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. | 11.472 | UI: chart-error-bars primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.490 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-error-bars.tsx` ships `<ChartErrorBars>` -- pure-SVG bar / scatter chart with vertical and (in scatter mode) horizontal error-bar overlays for confidence intervals. Each datum carries a required `y` value and optional `lower`/`upper` (or a single symmetric `error`) for the y-axis CI; in scatter mode it can also carry `x` plus optional `xLower`/`xUpper`/`xError` for the x-axis CI. Error bars render as T-shaped whiskers: a stem connecting `lower` to `upper` plus a short cap at each end. Mode toggles between bar (categorical-x with vertical T whiskers above/below the bar) and scatter (numeric-x, numeric-y with whiskers in either or both axes). CI resolution per axis: if both `lower` + `upper` are finite numbers they are used verbatim; else fall back to symmetric `+/- error` (only when error is finite + non-negative); else `hasError=false` and CI = `[value, value]`. Swap when lower > upper. Non-finite y skipped from the layout; non-finite / negative error ignored. Bar mode pulls `yMin` down to 0 when all values are positive so bars render from the baseline; scatter mode does not. Hover/focus on a mark sets the hovered id and opens a tooltip with label, the value (or `(x, y)` in scatter mode), and the formatted y/x CI ranges when present. Per-point click handler fires with `{point, layout}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per mark group (suppressed via `animate=false`). | 11.473 | UI: chart-histogram primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.491 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-histogram.tsx` ships `<ChartHistogram>` -- pure-SVG histogram with configurable bin count, count/density y-axis modes, an optional Gaussian-KDE density-curve overlay, and per-bar tooltips. Accepts a flat `number[]` of raw values; auto bin count defaults to Sturges' rule `ceil(log2(n) + 1)`. Distinct from `<ChartBar>` (11.438) which paints categorical bars and from `<ChartBoxplot>` (11.455) which summarises distributions instead of plotting the full bin frequencies. Bin range is auto-derived from finite values (collapsed range expands by +/-0.5); explicit `xMin` / `xMax` clamp the rendered range and drop out-of-range values. Non-finite values dropped before binning; the last bin is closed on the right edge so the maximum value still counts. y-axis modes: `count` (bar height proportional to `bin.count` over the visible peak) and `density` (`count / (totalFinite * step)` so the rendered area sums to 1 when range covers every value). KDE overlay: Gaussian kernel; bandwidth defaults to Silverman's rule (`1.06 * std * n^-0.2`; falls back to 1 when std <= 0 or n < 2); explicit `bandwidth` overrides. The curve is scaled back to the bar y-axis so it visually fits the histogram regardless of `yMode` -- in `count` mode the kernel density is multiplied by `totalFinite * binWidth` to match bar height. Hover/focus on a bar sets the hovered index and opens a tooltip with bin range, count, and density (each formatted). Per-bar click handler fires with `{bin, layout}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per bar group (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `values: readonly number[]` / `binCount?` / `xMin?` / `xMax?` / `yMode?` ('count'\|'density'; default 'count') / `width?` (560) / `height?` (320) / `padding?` (40) / `binGap?` (1) / `tickCount?` (5) / `showDensityCurve?` (false) / `densitySamples?` (64) / `bandwidth?` / `barColor?` ('#2563eb') / `densityColor?` ('#dc2626') / `showTooltip?` (true) / `showAxisTicks?` (true) / `showGrid?` (true) / `showXLabel?` (true) / `showYLabel?` (true) / `xLabel?` / `yLabel?` / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Histogram') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatRange?` / `onBinClick?({bin, layout})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_HISTOGRAM_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/TICK_COUNT/BIN_GAP/DENSITY_SAMPLES/BAR_COLOR/DENSITY_COLOR`; `getHistogramFiniteValues(values)` -- keeps finite numbers only; `getHistogramSturgesBinCount(n)` -- `ceil(log2(n) + 1)`; >= 1 for tiny / invalid input; `getHistogramBounds(values)` -- empty -> (0..1); collapsed range +/-0.5 expansion; `computeHistogramBins({values, binCount?, xMin?, xMax?})` -- canonical bin pass returning `{ index, start, end, count, density }[]`; empty -> []; sum of counts == finite-count when range covers all values; density sum * step ~= 1; clamps explicit binCount to >= 1; drops out-of-range values when xMin/xMax provided; `silvermanBandwidth(values)` -- 1 for tiny / non-finite / std=0; positive for varied input; `computeKernelDensity({values, xMin, xMax, samples?, bandwidth?})` -- returns `{ x, density }[]` evenly-spaced across [xMin, xMax]; non-positive bandwidth or `xMin == xMax` -> []; non-negative density; `getHistogramTicks(min, max, count?)` -- evenly-spaced; collapsed -> [min]; `computeHistogramLayout(input)` -- canonical layout returning `{ index, start, end, count, density, x, y, width, height, centerX, midValue }[]`; non-positive inner -> []; bar height scales with count or density (yMode-driven); `describeHistogram(values, bins, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Histogram of N values across M bins, range <min> to <max>. Peak bin <peakStart> to <peakEnd> with K values."; empty -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-histogram-aria-desc"` span; per-bar `<rect role="graphics-symbol" tabIndex={0}>` with aria-label `"Bin <range>: <count> values"` (count mode) / `"Bin <range>: density <density>"` (density mode). data-section on every node (chart-histogram / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -grid / -grid-line / -axes / -axis / -ticks / -tick / -tick-label / -x-label / -y-label / -bars / -bar / -rect / -density / -tooltip / -tooltip-range / -tooltip-count / -tooltip-density); root mirrors data-value-count, data-bin-count, data-y-mode, data-density-overlay, data-animate; bar groups mirror data-bin-index, data-bin-start, data-bin-end, data-bin-count, data-bin-density, data-hovered. 61 vitest cases (1 constants + 2 getHistogramFiniteValues + 2 getHistogramSturgesBinCount + 3 getHistogramBounds + 9 computeHistogramBins + 2 silvermanBandwidth + 4 computeKernelDensity + 3 getHistogramTicks + 5 computeHistogramLayout + 3 describeHistogram + 27 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented in docs/patches/11.473-ui-chart-histogram.md): adaptive / unequal-width bins (Bayesian Blocks, Freedman-Diaconis variable-width); multi-series / overlay histograms (host stacks instances); pre-binned input (v1 always re-bins); cumulative / step / ridge histogram variants; live streaming updates with incremental binning (v1 re-runs the bin pass per render). | 11.474 | UI: chart-ridge primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.492 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-ridge.tsx` ships `<ChartRidge>` -- pure-SVG ridgeline (joy plot) chart stacking multiple Gaussian-KDE density curves vertically with configurable overlap. Each input series produces a smoothed density curve; the curves are arranged top-to-bottom with optional overlap so neighbouring rows visually overlap to highlight distribution shape differences. Distinct from `<ChartViolin>` (11.456) -- violin paints a mirrored density per category as side-by-side vertical "violins", whereas ridge stacks one-sided densities vertically for multi-series visual comparison along a shared x axis. Density estimation: Gaussian KDE per series (`samples` evenly-spaced points across the rendered x range; default 64); bandwidth defaults to Silverman's rule (`1.06 * std * n^-0.2`; falls back to 1 when std=0 or n<2); explicit `bandwidth` overrides. Normalisation: per-row peak by default (every ridge fills its rowHeight regardless of absolute density, good for shape comparisons); `globalPeak=true` shares the maximum peak across rows so taller curves carry larger areas (good for absolute-density comparisons). Layout: `rawStride = innerH / N` so all rows fit; `rowHeight = rawStride * (1 + overlap)` (overlap clamped [0, 0.95]); `baselineY` walks down by rawStride and the curve paints from baseline upward (`baselineY - normalised * rowHeight`). Rows are painted in reverse-z order (last series first; series 0 sits visually on top); data attributes preserve original index for tests + callbacks. x range: auto-derived via `getRidgeBounds` with 4% padding on each side; collapsed range expands by +/-0.5; explicit `xMin`/`xMax` props override. Hover/focus on a row sets the hovered id, dims every other row to opacity 0.25, and opens a tooltip with label + finite-value count + peak density (formatted). Per-row click handler fires with `{series, layout}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per row group (suppressed via `animate=false`). Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_RIDGE_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/LABEL_WIDTH/OVERLAP/DENSITY_SAMPLES/TICK_COUNT/FILL_OPACITY/PALETTE`; `getRidgeDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; non-finite/negative -> color 0; `getRidgeFiniteValues(values)` -- keeps finite numbers only; `silvermanBandwidth(values)` -- 1 for tiny / collapsed; positive for varied input; `computeRidgeDensity({values, xMin, xMax, samples?, bandwidth?})` -- returns `{x, density}[]` evenly-spaced; tiny/collapsed -> []; non-negative density; `getRidgeBounds(series, padFactor?)` -- min/max across all series; empty -> (0..1); collapsed +/-0.5; padFactor expansion; `getRidgePeakDensity(density)` -- max density (empty -> 0); `getRidgeTicks(min, max, count?)` -- evenly-spaced; collapsed -> [min]; `computeRidgeLayout(input)` -- canonical layout returning `{ id, label, color, index, baselineY, topY, rowHeight, peakDensity, count, density, fillPath, linePath }[]`; non-positive inner / empty / collapsed -> []; `describeRidgeChart(series, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Ridgeline chart with N series, K values total. x range <xMin> to <xMax>."; empty/all-non-finite -> "No data".
