| 11.475 | UI: chart-marimekko primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.493 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-marimekko.tsx` ships `<ChartMarimekko>` -- pure-SVG Marimekko chart (variable-width stacked bars). Each column's *width* is proportional to its share of the grand total (`columnWidth = (columnTotal / grandTotal) * widthBudget`, where `widthBudget = innerW - (N - 1) * columnGap`); within each column, every visible series stacks vertically with cell heights proportional to the series's share of *that column's* total. Optional percentage labels render inside cells whose pixel area exceeds `labelMinArea` (default 280 px^2). Distinct from `<ChartStackedBar>` (11.468) which uses uniform column widths, and from `<ChartMosaic>` (11.457) which is similar but typically treats the data as a contingency table -- Marimekko emphasises composition across categories where the x axis is itself a value dimension. Non-positive / non-finite values are skipped from the layout entirely (they contribute neither width nor height nor a cell). Hidden series (controlled via `hiddenSeries` + `onHiddenSeriesChange` or uncontrolled via `defaultHiddenSeries`) drop their cells everywhere; column widths reproportion themselves to the remaining visible totals. `onSeriesToggle({series, hidden})` fires on legend click. Percentage labels paint at the cell center when `showPercentageLabels=true` AND the cell's pixel area >= `labelMinArea`; cells too small for a readable label automatically hide their text. `cellGap` is split half above + half below the cell so neighbours have a thin divider. Hover/focus on a cell sets the hovered key (`columnId::seriesId`) and opens a tooltip with the column + series labels, the formatted value, the share within the column, and the share of the overall grand total. Per-cell click handler fires with `{cell}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per cell group (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `columns: readonly ChartMarimekkoColumn[]` ({id, label, values: readonly number[]}) / `series: readonly ChartMarimekkoSeries[]` ({id, label, color?}) / `width?` (560) / `height?` (360) / `padding?` (36) / `cellGap?` (1) / `columnGap?` (2) / `labelMinArea?` (280) / `hiddenSeries?` / `defaultHiddenSeries?` / `onHiddenSeriesChange?` / `showLegend?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `showPercentageLabels?` (true) / `showColumnLabels?` (true) / `showColumnTotals?` (false) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Marimekko chart') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatPercent?` / `legendPlacement?` ('right'\|'bottom', default 'bottom') / `onCellClick?({cell})` / `onSeriesToggle?({series, hidden})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_MARIMEKKO_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/CELL_GAP/COLUMN_GAP/LABEL_MIN_AREA/PALETTE`; `getMarimekkoDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; non-finite/negative -> color 0; `getMarimekkoColumnTotal(column, hiddenIndices)` -- positive-finite sum; respects hidden; `getMarimekkoGrandTotal(columns, hiddenIndices)` -- sum across columns; `computeMarimekkoLayout({columns, series, hiddenSeries, innerW, innerH, padX, padY, cellGap, columnGap})` -- canonical layout returning per-column `{ id, index, label, total, share, x, y, width, height, cells }` where each cell is `{ columnId, columnIndex, seriesId, seriesIndex, value, columnTotal, columnShare, cellShare, overallShare, x, y, width, height, color, label, seriesLabel, columnLabel }`; non-positive inner / zero grand total / empty -> []; `describeMarimekkoChart(columns, series, hiddenSeries, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Marimekko chart with C columns and V visible series. Total <grand>."; empty / zero -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-marimekko-aria-desc"` span; per-cell `<rect role="graphics-symbol" tabIndex={0}>` with aria-label `"<columnLabel> / <seriesLabel>: <value> (<cellShare>% of column)"`; legend `<button aria-pressed>` per series + per-series `aria-label="Toggle <label>"`. data-section on every node (chart-marimekko / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -columns / -column / -cell / -rect / -cell-label / -column-label / -column-total / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-value / -tooltip-column / -tooltip-overall / -legend / -legend-item / -legend-button / -legend-swatch / -legend-label); root mirrors data-column-count, data-series-count, data-visible-series-count, data-cell-count, data-grand-total, data-animate; column groups mirror data-column-id, data-column-index, data-column-total, data-column-share, data-column-width; cell groups mirror data-column-id, data-series-id, data-series-index, data-cell-value, data-cell-color, data-cell-share, data-column-share, data-overall-share, data-hovered; legend items mirror data-series-id, data-series-hidden. 57 vitest cases (1 constants + 3 getMarimekkoDefaultColor + 3 getMarimekkoColumnTotal + 2 getMarimekkoGrandTotal + 14 computeMarimekkoLayout + 4 describeMarimekkoChart + 30 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. | 11.476 | UI: chart-slope primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.494 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-slope.tsx` ships `<ChartSlope>` -- pure-SVG slope / parallel-line chart for before-after comparison across two time points. Each item gets a connecting line from its `before` value on the left axis to its `after` value on the right axis. Direction colors (up green / down red / flat grey) make rate-of-change visually obvious at a glance. Distinct from `<ChartLine>` (11.439) which paints a continuous series over many x positions, and from `<ChartBullet>` (11.442) which compares a single value to a target range. Direction resolution via `getSlopeDirection`: when `after - before > epsilon` -> `up`; when `before - after > epsilon` -> `down`; else `flat`. `epsilon=0` (default) means any non-zero delta registers a direction; `epsilon > 0` widens the flat band so tiny noise is reported as flat. Non-finite values always resolve to `flat`. Color: per-item `color` always wins; otherwise the primitive picks `upColor` / `downColor` / `flatColor` based on the direction (default green / red / grey). Bounds auto-derived via `getSlopeBounds` across both endpoints (collapsed range expands by +/-0.5); `yMin` / `yMax` props override. Items with non-finite before OR after still appear in the layout but are flagged `isValid=false` and skipped from the painted line. Hover/focus on an item sets the hovered id, dims every other item to opacity 0.3 (focused slope dominates), and opens a tooltip with label, formatted before + after, signed delta, and the direction. Per-item click handler fires with `{item, layout}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per item group (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `items: readonly ChartSlopeItem[]` ({id, label, before, after, color?}) / `beforeLabel?` (default 'Before') / `afterLabel?` (default 'After') / `width?` (560) / `height?` (320) / `padding?` (40) / `labelGap?` (8) / `pointRadius?` (4) / `tickCount?` (5) / `yMin?` / `yMax?` / `epsilon?` (0) / `upColor?` ('#16a34a') / `downColor?` ('#dc2626') / `flatColor?` ('#64748b') / `showLeftLabels?` (true) / `showRightLabels?` (true) / `showLeftValues?` (true) / `showRightValues?` (true) / `showAxes?` (true) / `showAxisTicks?` (false) / `showGrid?` (false) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `showColumnHeaders?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Slope chart') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatLabel?` / `onItemClick?({item, layout})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_SLOPE_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/LABEL_GAP/POINT_RADIUS/TICK_COUNT/UP_COLOR/DOWN_COLOR/FLAT_COLOR`; `getSlopeDirection(before, after, epsilon?)` -- 'up'\|'down'\|'flat'; non-finite -> 'flat'; `getSlopePctChange(before, after)` -- `(after - before) / |before|`; zero-before with positive after -> +Infinity, with negative after -> -Infinity, both zero -> 0; non-finite -> 0; `getSlopeDirectionColor(direction, up, down, flat)` -- direction-to-color pick; `getSlopeBounds(items)` -- min/max across both endpoints; empty -> (0..1); non-finite skipped; collapsed +/-0.5; `getSlopeTicks(min, max, count?)` -- evenly-spaced; collapsed -> [min]; `computeSlopeLayout({items, bounds, innerW, innerH, padX, padY, upColor, downColor, flatColor, epsilon?})` -- canonical layout returning `{ id, label, index, color, direction, before, after, delta, pctChange, leftX, leftY, rightX, rightY, isValid }[]`; non-positive inner -> []; `describeSlopeChart(items, beforeLabel, afterLabel, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Slope chart from <before> to <after> comparing N items: U up, D down, F flat. Value range <yMin> to <yMax>."; empty/all-non-finite -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-slope-aria-desc"` span; per-line `<line role="graphics-symbol" tabIndex={0}>` with aria-label `"<label>: <before> -> <after> (<direction>)"`. data-section on every node (chart-slope / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -headers / -header / -grid / -grid-line / -axes / -axis / -ticks / -tick / -tick-label / -items / -item / -line / -point / -value / -label / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-before / -tooltip-after / -tooltip-delta); root mirrors data-item-count, data-visible-count, data-up-count, data-down-count, data-flat-count, data-animate; item groups mirror data-item-id, data-item-index, data-item-direction, data-item-before, data-item-after, data-item-delta, data-item-pct-change, data-item-color, data-hovered; endpoints mirror data-side="left"/"right". 60 vitest cases (1 constants + 3 getSlopeDirection + 4 getSlopePctChange + 3 getSlopeDirectionColor + 4 getSlopeBounds + 3 getSlopeTicks + 10 computeSlopeLayout + 4 describeSlopeChart + 28 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. | 11.477 | UI: chart-streamgraph primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.495 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-streamgraph.tsx` ships `<ChartStreamgraph>` -- pure-SVG streamgraph (stacked-area variant with selectable baseline) with smooth flow curves. Distinct from `<ChartStream>` (11.453) which is the simple centered variant -- ChartStreamgraph adds first-class **baseline algorithms** (`silhouette`, `wiggle`, `expand`, `zero`), **curve interpolation choice** (`cardinal`, `catmullRom`, `linear`, `step`), an explicit x-axis label track with `xLabels` + `formatXLabel`, and a `tension` parameter for the cardinal curve so an adopter can dial smoothness between piecewise-linear and full-Bezier. Baseline algorithms: `silhouette` (default) centres every sample around -total/2 producing the canonical streamgraph silhouette growing symmetrically up + down; `wiggle` minimises layer slope by walking the layers per sample (streamgraph minimum-wiggle algorithm; layers with all-zero totals inherit the previous offset so the baseline never jumps); `expand` is 100%-stacked (each sample's values rescale to [0, 1]; baseline stays at 0); `zero` is traditional flat-bottom stacked area. Curve interpolation: `cardinal` (default) uses tension to control smoothness (0 -> Catmull-Rom; 1 -> linear); `catmullRom` is the tension=0 special case; `linear` paints L commands between vertices; `step` paints square corners. Non-positive / non-finite raw values clamp to 0 so a series never inverts. Layers tile cleanly: layer N's `topValue` always equals layer N+1's `baseValue` at every sample. Hidden series (controlled or uncontrolled) drop from the layout entirely; remaining series reproportion across the stack. Hover/focus on a layer dims every other layer to opacity 0.3 (focused layer dominates) and opens a tooltip with the series label, sum of raw values across all samples, and sample count. `xLabels` (length = max series data length) drives x-axis tick labels; for >8 samples the primitive auto-thins to ~8 tick positions (first + last index always preserved) so labels never overlap. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per layer (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `series: readonly ChartStreamgraphSeries[]` ({id, label, data: readonly number[], color?}) / `xLabels?: readonly (string\|number)[]` / `baseline?` (default 'silhouette') / `curve?` (default 'cardinal') / `tension?` (default 0.5) / `width?` (640) / `height?` (280) / `padding?` (32) / `fillOpacity?` (0.7) / `hiddenSeries?` / `defaultHiddenSeries?` / `onHiddenSeriesChange?` / `showLegend?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `showXAxis?` (true) / `showXLabels?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Streamgraph') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatXLabel?` / `legendPlacement?` ('right'\|'bottom', default 'bottom') / `onLayerClick?({series, layer})` / `onSeriesToggle?({series, hidden})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_STREAMGRAPH_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/BASELINE/CURVE/TENSION/FILL_OPACITY/PALETTE`; `getStreamgraphDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; `getStreamgraphSampleCount(series)` -- largest data length; `getStreamgraphTotals(series, sampleCount)` -- sum per sample with non-positive/non-finite clamped; `computeStreamgraphBaseline(series, sampleCount, baseline)` -- canonical baseline computation per algorithm; `buildStreamgraphCurve(points, curve, startCommand, tension)` -- emits SVG path commands; empty -> ''; single point -> single M; `computeStreamgraphLayers({series, baseline, curve, tension, hidden, innerW, innerH, padX, padY})` -- canonical layout returning `{ layers, sampleCount, baselineValues, totals, yMin, yMax }` where each layer is `{ id, label, index, color, points: { x, baseValue, topValue, rawValue }[], topPath, bottomPath, areaPath }`; non-positive inner / empty / all-hidden -> empty result; `describeStreamgraphChart(series, hidden, baseline, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Streamgraph (<baseline>) with N series across M samples. Total <sum>, peak total <peak>."; empty / all-hidden -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-streamgraph-aria-desc"` span; per-area `<path role="graphics-symbol" tabIndex={0}>` with aria-label `"<label> stream layer"`; legend `<button aria-pressed>` per series + per-series `aria-label="Toggle <label>"`. data-section on every node (chart-streamgraph / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -layers / -layer / -area / -x-axis / -x-labels / -x-label / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-total / -tooltip-samples / -legend / -legend-item / -legend-button / -legend-swatch / -legend-label); root mirrors data-series-count, data-visible-count, data-sample-count, data-baseline, data-curve, data-animate; layer groups mirror data-series-id, data-series-index, data-series-color, data-hovered; legend items mirror data-series-id, data-series-hidden; x labels mirror data-sample-index. 62 vitest cases (1 constants + 3 getStreamgraphDefaultColor + 2 getStreamgraphSampleCount + 3 getStreamgraphTotals + 5 computeStreamgraphBaseline + 6 buildStreamgraphCurve + 11 computeStreamgraphLayers + 3 describeStreamgraphChart + 28 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented in docs/patches/11.477-ui-chart-streamgraph.md): negative values stacked below baseline (host normalises; values clamp to 0); smooth animated transitions between baseline / curve choices (snap v1; mount fade only); per-layer order control (host owns array; first series renders at the bottom of the stack); continuous time-axis ticks (v1 emits one label per sample index, auto-thinned). Reference /root/c4/arps-design-system-v1/. Branch c4/c4-mgr-auto. Worker auto-w425. Bump 1.11.495. |
| 11.478 | UI: chart-polar-area primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.496 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-polar-area.tsx` ships `<ChartPolarArea>` -- pure-SVG Nightingale rose / polar area chart. Every wedge gets an **equal angular slice** of the full circle (`2π / N`); **radius encodes value**. Default radius scaling is `sqrt` (so wedge area is proportional to value -- the honest Nightingale encoding since wedge area = `(angle/2) * r^2`); a `linear` mode is available for adopters who want radius itself proportional to value (over-emphasises larger values visually). Distinct from `<ChartPie>` (11.440) and `<ChartDonut>` (11.469) (where angle encodes value and radius is constant) and from `<ChartRadialBar>` (11.452) (which paints separate concentric rings per series rather than one wedge per category). Layout: `computePolarAreaLayout` carves the full circle into one wedge per visible item; each wedge occupies the same angular slice (`2π / N`, minus pad-angle per wedge when `padAngle > 0`). Default `startAngle = -pi/2` so the first wedge begins at 12 o'clock. Non-positive / non-finite values render no wedge (radius = 0). `maxValue` prop overrides the auto-derived peak so multiple instances can share a comparable radial scale. Hover/focus on a wedge dims every other wedge to opacity 0.3 (focused wedge dominates) and opens a tooltip with label, formatted value, and the percentage ratio against `maxValue`. Axis rings paint at every tick value (one per evenly-spaced step from 0..maxValue); axis labels paint at the top of every ring (the 0 ring is skipped). Optional in-wedge labels at the centroid (62% radius) when `showWedgeLabels=true` and the rendered radius is large enough. Legend (when present): focusable `<button aria-pressed>` per wedge; controlled (`hiddenWedges` + `onHiddenWedgesChange`) and uncontrolled (`defaultHiddenWedges`); toggling fires `onWedgeToggle({wedge, hidden})` with the next state. Per-wedge click handler fires with `{wedge, layout}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per wedge (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `wedges: readonly ChartPolarAreaWedge[]` ({id, label, value, color?}) / `width?` (360) / `height?` (360) / `padding?` (32) / `startAngle?` (-pi/2) / `padAngle?` (0) / `radiusMode?` ('sqrt'\|'linear'; default 'sqrt') / `maxValue?` / `tickCount?` (4) / `fillOpacity?` (0.7) / `hiddenWedges?` / `defaultHiddenWedges?` / `onHiddenWedgesChange?` / `showLegend?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `showAxisRings?` (true) / `showAxisLabels?` (true) / `showWedgeLabels?` (false) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Polar area chart') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `legendPlacement?` ('right'\|'bottom', default 'bottom') / `onWedgeClick?({wedge, layout})` / `onWedgeToggle?({wedge, hidden})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_POLAR_AREA_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/START_ANGLE/PAD_ANGLE/TICK_COUNT/RADIUS_MODE/FILL_OPACITY/PALETTE`; `getPolarAreaDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; non-finite/negative -> color 0; `polarToCartesian(cx, cy, r, angle)` -- standard SVG y-down; `getPolarAreaMaxValue(wedges)` -- largest finite value; 0 for empty; non-finite skipped; `getPolarAreaRadius(value, maxValue, outerRadius, mode)` -- 0 for non-positive value or non-positive max; sqrt mode uses `sqrt(ratio) * outerRadius`; linear mode uses `ratio * outerRadius`; clamps ratio over 1 to the outer radius; `getPolarAreaTicks(max, count?)` -- evenly-spaced 0..max; non-positive max -> [0]; count clamped >= 2; `computePolarAreaLayout({wedges, hidden, cx, cy, outerRadius, startAngle, padAngle, radiusMode, maxValueOverride?})` -- canonical layout returning `{ wedges, maxValue }` where each wedge is `{ id, label, index, value, color, startAngle, endAngle, midAngle, outerRadius, ratio, path, midLabelX, midLabelY }`; empty / all-hidden / zero-max -> `{ wedges: [], maxValue: 0 }`; `describePolarAreaChart(wedges, hidden, radiusMode, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Polar area chart (<mode> radius) with N wedges, peak value <peak>."; empty / all-hidden -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-polar-area-aria-desc"` span; per-path `<path role="graphics-symbol" tabIndex={0}>` with aria-label `"<label>: <value>"`; legend `<button aria-pressed>` per wedge + per-wedge `aria-label="Toggle <label>"`. data-section on every node (chart-polar-area / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -rings / -ring / -wedges / -wedge / -path / -wedge-label / -axis-labels / -axis-label / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-value / -tooltip-ratio / -legend / -legend-item / -legend-button / -legend-swatch / -legend-label); root mirrors data-wedge-count, data-visible-count, data-max-value, data-radius-mode, data-animate; wedge groups mirror data-wedge-id, data-wedge-index, data-wedge-value, data-wedge-ratio, data-wedge-color, data-wedge-radius, data-hovered; legend items mirror data-wedge-id, data-wedge-hidden; axis rings + labels mirror data-tick-value. 58 vitest cases (1 constants + 3 getPolarAreaDefaultColor + 3 polarToCartesian + 3 getPolarAreaMaxValue + 5 getPolarAreaRadius + 3 getPolarAreaTicks + 11 computePolarAreaLayout + 3 describePolarAreaChart + 26 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented in docs/patches/11.478-ui-chart-polar-area.md): stacked polar wedges with multi-series ring per wedge (one wedge per item v1); animated transitions on data / radiusMode change (snap v1; mount fade only); custom kernel for the angular smoothing (no smoothing v1); polar tick marks per angle (use `<ChartRadar>` axes for tick labels around the perimeter); negative values (Nightingale requires positive areas; non-positive skipped). | 11.479 | UI: chart-treemap-squarified primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.497 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-treemap-squarified.tsx` ships `<ChartTreemapSquarified>` -- pure-SVG **squarified** treemap. Implements the Bruls/Huijsen/van Wijk (2000) layout: values sorted descending and greedily packed into rows along the **short side** of the remaining free rectangle so the worst-case cell aspect ratio is minimised at every step. Distinct from `<ChartTreemap>` (11.444) which typically uses slice-and-dice where cells inherit the parent's strong aspect ratio (one tall column with thin slivers); squarified trades a small amount of value-order locality for much more readable rectangles. Algorithm: 1) drop non-positive / non-finite values, sort remaining by value descending; 2) normalise areas so they sum to `innerW * innerH`; 3) greedy row-packing -- for each item, try adding it to the current row; compute the worst aspect ratio of the row with vs without the item; keep the row when adding makes it better, otherwise lay out the row and start a new row; 4) rows always lay along the **short side** of the remaining free rectangle; 5) each cell carries an `aspectRatio` field so adopters can inspect per-cell quality. The canonical sort preserves the original index so click + ref payloads stay correlated. `cellGap` is split half above and half below each cell so neighbours have a thin divider; total cell area equals `innerW * innerH` when `cellGap=0`, and cell areas are proportional to `value / total`. Hover/focus on a cell sets the hovered id and opens a tooltip with label, formatted value, share against grand total, and the computed aspect ratio. Per-cell click handler fires with `{item, layout}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per cell group (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `items: readonly ChartTreemapSquarifiedItem[]` ({id, label, value, color?}) / `width?` (560) / `height?` (360) / `padding?` (24) / `cellGap?` (2) / `labelMinArea?` (360 px^2) / `fillOpacity?` (0.85) / `showLegend?` (false) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `showLabels?` (true) / `showValues?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Squarified treemap') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatPercent?` / `legendPlacement?` ('right'\|'bottom') / `onCellClick?({item, layout})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_TREEMAP_SQUARIFIED_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/CELL_GAP/LABEL_MIN_AREA/FILL_OPACITY/PALETTE`; `getTreemapSquarifiedDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; non-finite/negative -> color 0; `sortTreemapSquarifiedDesc(items)` -- canonical desc sort returning `{ item, originalIndex }[]`; drops non-positive / non-finite; `getTreemapSquarifiedTotal(items)` -- positive finite sum; `computeTreemapSquarifiedLayout({items, innerW, innerH, padX, padY, cellGap})` -- canonical squarified layout returning `{ id, label, index, value, share, color, x, y, width, height, aspectRatio }[]`; non-positive inner / empty / zero total -> []; `describeTreemapSquarifiedChart(items, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Squarified treemap with N cells, total <total>. Largest cell <label> <value>."; empty / zero -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-treemap-squarified-aria-desc"` span; per-rect `role="graphics-symbol"` + `tabIndex={0}` + aria-label `"<label>: <value> (<percent>)"`. data-section on every node (chart-treemap-squarified / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -cells / -cell / -rect / -label / -value / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-value / -tooltip-share / -tooltip-aspect / -legend / -legend-item / -legend-row / -legend-swatch / -legend-label); root mirrors data-item-count, data-cell-count, data-total, data-worst-aspect-ratio, data-animate; cell groups mirror data-cell-id, data-cell-index, data-cell-value, data-cell-share, data-cell-color, data-cell-aspect-ratio, data-hovered. 49 vitest cases (1 constants + 3 getTreemapSquarifiedDefaultColor + 3 sortTreemapSquarifiedDesc + 2 getTreemapSquarifiedTotal + 13 computeTreemapSquarifiedLayout (incl. worst-aspect-ratio < 8 quality test that proves the squarification actually works) + 2 describeTreemapSquarifiedChart + 25 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented in docs/patches/11.479-ui-chart-treemap-squarified.md): nested / hierarchical treemap with parent groups (v1 is flat; host composes nested instances or uses `<ChartTreemap>`); animated transitions on data change (snap v1; mount fade only); alternative quality metrics like `(w-h)^2 / max(w,h)^2` (v1 uses canonical `max(w/h, h/w)` ratio); per-cell border / corner radius (v1 paints rectangles only). Reference /root/c4/arps-design-system-v1/. Branch c4/c4-mgr-auto. Worker auto-w425. Bump 1.11.497. |
| 11.480 | UI: chart-funnel-area primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.498 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-funnel-area.tsx` ships `<ChartFunnelArea>` -- pure-SVG **area-funnel** variant where each stage's **vertical height is proportional to its value share** and the funnel walls taper smoothly from the full width at the top to a configurable neck-ratio width at the bottom. Distinct from `<ChartFunnel>` (11.443) which sizes each trapezoid's *width* by value with equal heights; in ChartFunnelArea every stage is a wide band and its area (height x mean width) is proportional to value, matching the common "stage by share" reading in analytics dashboards. Layout: heights are `(value / total) * heightBudget` (heightBudget = `innerH - (N-1)*stageGap`); width tapers linearly with cumulative share -- `width = topWidthFull + (bottomWidthFull - topWidthFull) * cumulativeShare`, where `bottomWidthFull = innerW * neckRatio`. Each stage carries top/bottom widths at its boundaries so the previous stage's bottom width equals the next stage's top width (continuous funnel walls). `neckRatio` clamped to [0, 1] (0 collapses to a point; 1 is a straight column). Conversion rate per stage `i > 0` is `value[i] / value[i-1]` (clamped to 0 when previous is <= 0 or non-finite). First stage's conversion = 1, drop = 0. Optional in-trapezoid label + value text renders at the centroid when stage height >= `labelMinHeight`. Optional conversion-rate badge to the right of each stage `i > 0` when `showConversionRates=true`. Non-positive / non-finite values still occupy a slot but render with height 0 so funnel geometry stays continuous. Hover/focus dims other stages to opacity 0.4 and opens a tooltip with label, value, share against total, and the conversion rate (omitted for first stage). Per-stage click handler fires with `{stage, layout}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per stage (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `stages: readonly ChartFunnelAreaStage[]` ({id, label, value, color?}) / `width?` (480) / `height?` (360) / `padding?` (32) / `neckRatio?` (0.3) / `stageGap?` (2) / `labelMinHeight?` (18) / `fillOpacity?` (0.85) / `showLabels?` (true) / `showValues?` (true) / `showConversionRates?` (false) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `showLegend?` (false) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Area funnel chart') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatPercent?` / `legendPlacement?` ('right'\|'bottom', default 'bottom') / `onStageClick?({stage, layout})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_FUNNEL_AREA_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/NECK_RATIO/STAGE_GAP/LABEL_MIN_HEIGHT/FILL_OPACITY/PALETTE`; `getFunnelAreaDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; non-finite/negative -> color 0; `getFunnelAreaTotalValue(stages)` -- positive finite sum; empty -> 0; `getFunnelAreaConversionRate(current, previous)` -- current/previous; previous<=0 -> 0; non-finite -> 0; `computeFunnelAreaLayout({stages, innerW, innerH, padX, padY, neckRatio, stageGap})` -- canonical layout returning `{ id, label, index, value, share, cumulativeShare, color, yTop, yBottom, topWidth, bottomWidth, centerX, height, path, conversionRate, dropRate }[]`; non-positive inner / empty / zero total -> []; `describeFunnelAreaChart(stages, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Area funnel with N stages, total <total>. Top stage <first.label> <first.value>, end stage <last.label> <last.value> (<conversion> conversion)."; empty / zero -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-funnel-area-aria-desc"` span; per-path `role="graphics-symbol"` + `tabIndex={0}` + aria-label `"<label>: <value> (<percent> of total)"`. data-section on every node (chart-funnel-area / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -stages / -stage / -path / -label / -value / -conversion / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-value / -tooltip-share / -tooltip-conversion / -legend / -legend-item / -legend-row / -legend-swatch / -legend-label); root mirrors data-stage-count, data-visible-count, data-total, data-neck-ratio, data-animate; stage groups mirror data-stage-id, data-stage-index, data-stage-value, data-stage-share, data-stage-color, data-stage-conversion, data-stage-drop, data-hovered. 57 vitest cases (1 constants + 3 getFunnelAreaDefaultColor + 3 getFunnelAreaTotalValue + 4 getFunnelAreaConversionRate + 16 computeFunnelAreaLayout (incl. invariants: heights proportional to share, widths taper monotonically, prev.bottomWidth == next.topWidth) + 2 describeFunnelAreaChart + 28 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. | 11.481 | UI: chart-pictogram primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.499 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-pictogram.tsx` ships `<ChartPictogram>` -- pure-SVG pictogram (isotype) chart that uses repeated icons to represent quantities. Each row paints `value / unitValue` icons in a left-to-right grid, with the final icon partially filled when the value is fractional (clipped via per-row `<clipPath>` so the fractional portion is visually meaningful). Distinct from every other chart-* primitive: this is the canonical Otto-Neurath isotype presentation where the **count of glyphs** -- not a continuous bar or area -- carries the quantitative meaning. Built-in icon shapes: `circle` (default), `square`, `rounded`, `star`, `triangle`, `hexagon`, `person`. A custom SVG path (starting with `M`) can be passed in place of a shape name; the path is used verbatim. Empty (background) icons paint behind every glyph at `emptyOpacity` (default 0.18) so each slot is visible even when empty -- 7-of-10 lights filled, not 7 lights floating. Icons-per-row is auto-computed from the available inner width minus the label gutter divided by `iconSize + iconGap`; long rows wrap automatically into additional visual rows. Hover/focus on a row sets the hovered id, dims other rows to opacity 0.4, and opens a tooltip with label, formatted value, and the icon count. Per-row label (left-anchored at the label gutter) + per-row count badge (right of the glyph block) render by default. Per-row click handler fires with `{row, layout}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per row (suppressed via `animate=false`). Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_PICTOGRAM_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/ICON_SIZE/ICON_GAP/ROW_GAP/LABEL_WIDTH/UNIT_VALUE/ICON_SHAPE/EMPTY_OPACITY/PALETTE`; `getPictogramDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; non-finite/negative -> color 0; `getPictogramIconCount(value, unitValue)` -- canonical full/fractional/total count; non-positive / non-finite value or unitValue -> zero; `buildPictogramIconPath(shape, size)` -- emits closed M..Z SVG path per shape (circle uses A commands, square uses L, rounded uses L+A, triangle has 3 vertices, hexagon has 6, star has 10 segments, person combines head + body + arms + legs); custom M-prefixed paths returned verbatim; size <= 0 -> ''; `computePictogramLayout({rows, unitValue, iconSize, iconGap, rowGap, labelWidth, innerW, padX, padY, defaultIcon})` -- canonical layout returning `{ id, label, index, value, color, icon, totalIcons, fullIcons, fractionalIcon, iconsPerRow, visualRows, rowY, rowHeight, icons }[]` where each icon is `{ index, x, y, fill }`; non-positive innerW / empty rows -> []; non-positive value records the row with 0 icons; `describePictogramChart(rows, unitValue, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Pictogram chart with N rows, total <total> across K icons (each icon = <unitValue>)."; empty / all-zero -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-pictogram-aria-desc"` span; per-row icon group `role="graphics-symbol"` + `tabIndex={0}` + aria-label `"<label>: <value> (<count> icons)"`. data-section on every node (chart-pictogram / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -rows / -row / -row-label / -icons / -icon / -icon-empty / -icon-fill / -count / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-value / -tooltip-icons / -legend / -legend-item / -legend-row / -legend-swatch / -legend-label); root mirrors data-row-count, data-visible-row-count, data-icon-count, data-unit-value, data-total-value, data-default-icon, data-animate; row groups mirror data-row-id, data-row-index, data-row-value, data-row-color, data-row-icon-count, data-row-full-icons, data-row-fractional-icon, data-row-visual-rows, data-hovered; icon groups mirror data-icon-index, data-icon-fill (0..1). 59 vitest cases (1 constants + 3 getPictogramDefaultColor + 4 getPictogramIconCount + 9 buildPictogramIconPath + 10 computePictogramLayout + 3 describePictogramChart + 29 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. | 11.482 | UI: chart-spider-web primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.500 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-spider-web.tsx` ships `<ChartSpiderWeb>` -- pure-SVG **circular hub-spoke** layout for hub-spoke node visualization. One hub node anchors the centre; every remaining node spreads evenly on a perimeter circle. Hub-spoke edges paint as radial spokes from the hub outward; spoke-to-spoke edges paint as straight lines across the chart. Optional `groupRings=true` stacks spokes on per-group concentric rings so nodes in the same `group` field share a radius -- each group gets its own concentric ring; the ring radius steps evenly from `outerRadius / N_groups` to `outerRadius`. Distinct from `<ChartNetwork>` (11.454, force-directed), `<ChartChord>` (11.462, chord around a ring), `<ChartArcDiagram>` (11.463, baseline + arcs), `<ChartRadar>` (11.445, multi-axis polygon), and `<ChartRadarSpider>` (11.464, axis-wedge variant): this primitive is specifically the **hub-centric topology** display where a single node dominates and others orbit. Hub selection: `hubId` prop names the centre node; if absent or not in `nodes`, the first node in the array is the hub. Default `startAngle = -pi/2` so the first spoke sits at 12 o'clock. Per-node radius scales by `sqrt(weight)`; per-edge stroke width clamps to [0.8, 4] px from `edge.weight`. Hover/focus on a node sets the hovered id, dims unrelated nodes to opacity 0.3 and unrelated edges to opacity 0.18 (`highlightOnHover=true` by default), and opens a tooltip with label, degree, and group. Hover on an edge keeps the edge fully rendered while siblings dim only when a node is also hovered; tooltip surfaces src-tgt + weight. Optional concentric dashed rings (`showRings=true`) paint at per-group radii to make the hub-spoke geometry obvious. Per-node + per-edge click handlers fire with full payloads. Edges referencing unknown ids are silently dropped. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per node + edge (suppressed via `animate=false`). | 11.483 | UI: chart-sunburst primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.501 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-sunburst.tsx` ships `<ChartSunburst>` -- pure-SVG **sunburst** (radial hierarchical) chart with **click-to-zoom into branches**. Each ring is one level of the hierarchy; each arc encodes its share of its parent. Clicking any arc makes it the new focus -- its subtree expands to fill the full 2pi and every other branch is hidden; clicking the center disc zooms back out one level toward the root. Value resolution (`getSunburstNodeValue`): leaves use their explicit `value`; non-leaf nodes prefer the sum of their children's values (an explicit parent `value` is treated as a fallback only when child totals collapse to 0); childless nodes without a value contribute 0. Layout (`computeSunburstLayout`): each level of the focus subtree gets its own ring; ring count = `maxDepth - focusDepth + 1`; ring width = `(outerRadius - centerRadius) / ringCount`; inner ring renders the focus node spanning the full 2pi; child rings stack outward; each child's angular span is proportional to its share of the parent. Outside the focus subtree, no arcs render. Click-to-zoom is controlled (`focusPath` + `onFocusPathChange`) or uncontrolled (`defaultFocusPath`); arc click fires `onArcClick({node, becameFocus})`. Center disc click zooms out by one level (last element of focus path dropped); already-at-root center clicks are a no-op. Center disc has `role="button"` + `tabIndex={0}` so keyboard users can zoom out. Arc labels paint at the centroid when arc angular span >= `labelMinArc` (default 0.18 rad) AND ring is at least 14 px tall. Hover/focus on an arc opens a tooltip with the full breadcrumb path, formatted value, share against focus value, and share of overall total. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per arc (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `root: ChartSunburstNode \| null` ({id, label, value?, color?, children?}) / `width?` (400) / `height?` (400) / `padding?` (24) / `centerRadius?` (36) / `fillOpacity?` (0.85) / `labelMinArc?` (0.18 rad) / `focusPath?` / `defaultFocusPath?` / `onFocusPathChange?` / `showCenterLabel?` (true) / `showLabels?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Sunburst chart') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatPercent?` / `fallbackColor?` ('#94a3b8') / `onArcClick?({node, becameFocus})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_SUNBURST_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/CENTER_RADIUS/FILL_OPACITY/LABEL_MIN_ARC/PALETTE`; `getSunburstDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; `polarToCartesian(cx, cy, r, angle)` -- standard SVG y-down; `getSunburstNodeValue(node)` -- canonical leaf/parent value resolution; `flattenSunburstHierarchy(root)` -- depth-first flatten returning `{ id, label, depth, parentId, path, value, isLeaf, originalIndex, color? }[]`; null root -> []; `getSunburstMaxDepth(flat)` -- deepest depth; empty -> 0; `computeSunburstLayout({root, focusPath, cx, cy, outerRadius, centerRadius, fallbackColor})` -- canonical layout returning `{ arcs, flat, focusNode, focusValue, maxDepth, ringWidth }`; null root / non-positive outer / zero focus value -> empty arcs; unknown focus path falls back to root; `describeSunburstChart(root, focusPath, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Sunburst chart with N nodes across L levels, total <total>. Focused on <focus.label> (depth D)."; null root / zero -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-sunburst-aria-desc"` span; per-arc `<path role="graphics-symbol" tabIndex={0}>` with aria-label `"<label>: <value> (<percent>)"`; center disc `role="button"` + `tabIndex={0}` with aria-label `"Zoom out from <focus>"` or `"Focused on <focus>"`. data-section on every node (chart-sunburst / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -arcs / -arc / -path / -arc-label / -center / -center-disc / -center-label / -center-value / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-value / -tooltip-share / -tooltip-global); root mirrors data-node-count, data-arc-count, data-focus-id, data-focus-depth, data-max-depth, data-animate; arc groups mirror data-arc-id, data-arc-depth, data-arc-parent, data-arc-value, data-arc-share, data-arc-global-share, data-arc-color, data-arc-is-focus, data-hovered. 52 vitest cases (1 constants + 1 getSunburstDefaultColor + 1 polarToCartesian + 4 getSunburstNodeValue + 2 flattenSunburstHierarchy + 2 getSunburstMaxDepth + 12 computeSunburstLayout (incl. zoom invariants: zoomed subtree spans full 2pi; click-to-zoom transitions render only descendants) + 2 describeSunburstChart + 27 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. New `web/src/components/ui/chart-icicle.tsx` ships `<ChartIcicle>` -- pure-SVG **icicle** chart, the rectangular variant of `<ChartSunburst>` (11.483). Each level of the hierarchy is a band; within a band, sibling rectangles tile the parent's extent with sizes proportional to their share of the parent. Two orientations: `horizontal` (root at top, children below) or `vertical` (root at left, children to the right). Click any cell to make it the new focus -- the focus subtree expands to fill the full canvas extent. A breadcrumb above the canvas (`<nav aria-label="Icicle breadcrumb">` with one `<button aria-label="Zoom to <label>">` per ancestor) lets adopters jump back to any ancestor. Value resolution: leaves use their explicit `value` (positive finite); non-leaf nodes prefer the sum of their children's values, falling back to the explicit value only when child totals collapse to 0. Layout: bands = `maxDepth - focusDepth + 1`; horizontal band size = `height / bands`; vertical band size = `width / bands`; focus cell spans full extent of the band axis; child cells stack along the orthogonal axis with sizes proportional to share. `cellGap` is split half on each side of every cell. Click-to-zoom controlled (`focusPath` + `onFocusPathChange`) or uncontrolled (`defaultFocusPath`); cell click fires `onCellClick({cell, becameFocus})`; breadcrumb click rewinds focus to that ancestor. Cell labels paint inside when rendered dimensions exceed both `labelMinWidth` (default 36) and `labelMinHeight` (default 14). Hover/focus opens tooltip with breadcrumb path, formatted value, share against focus value, and share of overall total. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per cell (suppressed via `animate=false`). | 11.485 | UI: chart-circle-packing primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.503 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-circle-packing.tsx` ships `<ChartCirclePacking>` -- pure-SVG **hierarchical circle packing**. Every node in the input hierarchy becomes a circle; parent circles enclose their children; child radii are proportional to `sqrt(value)` so circle *area* tracks value (the standard area-honest encoding). Distinct from `<ChartTreemap>` (11.444) / `<ChartTreemapSquarified>` (11.479) (rectangular nesting), `<ChartSunburst>` (11.483) (radial banded), and `<ChartIcicle>` (11.484) (rectangular banded) -- this primitive is the **packed-circles** layout that emphasises hierarchy + relative size at a glance. Value resolution: leaves use explicit `value`; non-leaf nodes prefer sum of children (fallback to explicit only when child totals collapse to 0). Layout: root placed at `(cx, cy)` with outer radius; for each parent, children are packed via a **front-chain algorithm** (Wang et al. 2006 style) -- place first two children tangent to each other; place the third tangent to the first two; for each subsequent child, walk the circular "front" of boundary circles and try every adjacent pair `(a, b)`; place the new circle tangent to both at the position closest to the centroid; reject if it intersects any other front circle; otherwise insert into the front between `a` and `b`. The packed cluster's minimum enclosing circle is computed and the whole cluster is translated + scaled so it sits inside the parent's circle with `childPadding` clearance. Non-positive / non-finite values are dropped from the layout. Non-overlap is enforced within ~1 px tolerance: siblings are mutually non-overlapping; every child fits inside its parent. Labels: leaves (and the focused root) get labels by default; setting `showLeafLabelsOnly=false` labels every visible circle; labels paint at the centroid with font size scaled to the radius (clamped to [9, 13] px). Hover/focus opens a tooltip with the full breadcrumb path, formatted value, and share against the root. Per-circle click handler fires with `{circle}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per circle (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `root: ChartCirclePackingNode \| null` ({id, label, value?, color?, children?}) / `width?` (400) / `height?` (400) / `padding?` (16) / `childPadding?` (4) / `fillOpacity?` (0.6) / `labelMinRadius?` (16) / `showLabels?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `showLeafLabelsOnly?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Circle packing chart') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatPercent?` / `fallbackColor?` ('#94a3b8') / `onCircleClick?({circle})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_CIRCLE_PACKING_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/CHILD_PADDING/FILL_OPACITY/LABEL_MIN_RADIUS/PALETTE`; `getCirclePackingDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; `getCirclePackingNodeValue(node)` -- canonical value resolution; `flattenCirclePackingHierarchy(root)` -- depth-first flatten returning `{ id, label, depth, parentId, path, value, isLeaf, color? }[]`; null -> []; `packCirclesFrontChain(radii)` -- canonical Wang et al. front-chain packing returning `{ x, y, r }[]` (one per input radius, zero placeholder for non-positive / non-finite inputs; siblings non-overlapping within tolerance); `getCirclePackingEnclosingCircle(circles)` -- returns minimum-enclosing-circle approximation; empty -> zero; encloses every input circle; `computeCirclePackingLayout({root, cx, cy, radius, childPadding, fallbackColor})` -- canonical layout returning `{ circles, flat, rootValue }`; null / non-positive radius / zero rootValue -> empty circles; `describeCirclePackingChart(root, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Circle packing chart with N nodes across L levels, total <total>."; null / zero -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-circle-packing-aria-desc"` span; per-circle `<circle role="graphics-symbol" tabIndex={0}>` with aria-label `"<label>: <value> (<percent>)"`. data-section on every node (chart-circle-packing / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -circles / -circle / -shape / -label / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-value / -tooltip-share); root mirrors data-node-count, data-circle-count, data-root-value, data-animate; circle groups mirror data-circle-id, data-circle-depth, data-circle-parent, data-circle-value, data-circle-share, data-circle-color, data-circle-radius, data-circle-is-leaf, data-circle-is-focus, data-hovered. 50 vitest cases (1 constants + 1 getCirclePackingDefaultColor + 4 getCirclePackingNodeValue + 2 flattenCirclePackingHierarchy + 6 packCirclesFrontChain (incl. non-overlap invariants for 3 + many radii) + 3 getCirclePackingEnclosingCircle + 9 computeCirclePackingLayout (incl. invariants: every child fits inside its parent + siblings don't overlap) + 2 describeCirclePackingChart + 22 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented in docs/patches/11.485-ui-chart-circle-packing.md): click-to-zoom into focus subtree (v1 is read-only; host composes state if needed); drag-to-reorder children (v1 paints in array order; host pre-sorts); animated transitions on data change (snap v1; mount fade only); non-circular boundary like ellipse / polygon packing (v1 is canonical circle packing). Reference /root/c4/arps-design-system-v1/. Branch c4/c4-mgr-auto. Worker auto-w425. Bump 1.11.503. |
| 11.486 | UI: chart-dendrogram primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.504 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-dendrogram.tsx` ships `<ChartDendrogram>` -- pure-SVG **dendrogram** (tree) chart with right-angle (elbow) links between parent and child nodes and leaf labels. Four orientations: `right` (root left, leaves right; default), `down` (root top, leaves bottom), `left` (root right, leaves left), `up` (root bottom, leaves top). Distinct from the other hierarchical primitives -- `<ChartSunburst>` (11.483) is radial banded, `<ChartIcicle>` (11.484) is rectangular banded, `<ChartCirclePacking>` (11.485) packs nested circles, `<ChartTreemap>` / `<ChartTreemapSquarified>` nest rectangles -- this primitive is the classic **node-link tree** used for taxonomies, clustering, and file-tree visualisations. Layout (`computeDendrogramLayout`): walk the input tree depth-first to assign each leaf a unique `leafIndex` (0..N-1 in DFS order); leaves placed at `leafIndex * leafStep` along the leaf axis and at the deepest depth-axis offset (with `leafLabelReserve` px reserved on the leaf side for labels); each internal node sits at the centroid of its children along the leaf axis and at its own depth offset along the depth axis. Right/left orientations use x for depth and y for leaves; down/up orientations use y for depth and x for leaves. Links use `buildDendrogramElbowPath` to draw a two-segment right-angle path from parent to child -- for horizontal orientations the elbow is at `(targetDepth, sourceLeafCoord)`; for vertical orientations the elbow is at `(sourceLeafCoord, targetDepth)`. Single-leaf trees centre the leaf at canvas midpoint along the leaf axis. Per-node `color` always wins; otherwise leaves use `leafColor` (default '#2563eb') and internals use `internalColor` (default '#64748b'). Leaf labels render anchored away from the leaf axis (`start` for `right`, `end` for `left`, `middle` for `down`/`up`); internal labels hidden by default; `showInternalLabels=true` enables them at the node centroid with a small upward offset. Hover/focus on a node opens a tooltip with label, depth, and either `leaf` (for leaves) or `<leafCount> leaves` (for internal nodes); hover/focus on a link opens a link tooltip showing `<source> -> <target>` only when no node is also hovered. Per-node + per-link click handlers fire with full payloads. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per node + link (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `root: ChartDendrogramNode \| null` ({id, label, color?, children?}) / `width?` (560) / `height?` (360) / `padding?` (24) / `orientation?` ('right'\|'down'\|'left'\|'up'; default 'right') / `labelGap?` (6) / `leafLabelReserve?` (80) / `nodeRadius?` (3) / `leafRadius?` (4) / `leafColor?` / `internalColor?` / `linkColor?` ('#94a3b8') / `showLeafLabels?` (true) / `showInternalLabels?` (false) / `showNodes?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Dendrogram') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatLabel?` / `onNodeClick?({node})` / `onLinkClick?({link})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_DENDROGRAM_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/LABEL_GAP/NODE_RADIUS/LEAF_RADIUS/ORIENTATION/LINK_COLOR/LEAF_COLOR/INTERNAL_COLOR`; `getDendrogramDefaultColor(isLeaf, leafColor, internalColor)` -- leaf vs internal color pick; `flattenDendrogramHierarchy(root)` -- depth-first flatten returning `{ id, label, depth, parentId, path, isLeaf, color? }[]`; null -> []; `getDendrogramLeaves(root)` -- filtered leaves in DFS order; `getDendrogramMaxDepth(flat)` -- deepest depth; `buildDendrogramElbowPath(source, target, orientation)` -- two-segment elbow SVG path; `computeDendrogramLayout({root, orientation, width, height, padX, padY, labelGap, leafLabelReserve, leafColor, internalColor})` -- canonical layout returning `{ nodes, links, flat, leafCount, maxDepth }`; null / non-positive dims -> empty; `describeDendrogramChart(root, orientation)` -- ARIA summary "Dendrogram (<orientation>) with N nodes, L leaves, depth D."; null -> "No data". | 11.487 | UI: chart-tree-radial primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.505 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-tree-radial.tsx` ships `<ChartTreeRadial>` -- pure-SVG **radial tree** layout, the polar variant of `<ChartDendrogram>` (11.486). The root sits at the centre, leaves radiate out at the perimeter, and each level of the hierarchy lives at a fixed radius. Three link styles connect parents to children: `curve` (default; smooth cubic bezier in polar space with both control points midway between source and target angles), `elbow` (arc along the parent's radius from source angle to target angle, then a radial line out to the child), or `line` (straight cartesian line). `elbow` with zero source radius falls back to `line`. Layout (`computeTreeRadialLayout`): walk DFS to assign each leaf a unique `leafIndex` (0..N-1); each leaf placed at angle `startAngle + leafIndex * (2pi / leafCount)` and radius `outerRadius`; each internal node sits at the *mean* of its children's angles at radius `depth * depthStep` where `depthStep = outerRadius / maxDepth`. The root therefore lives at radius 0 (centre). `outerRadius` derived from `min(innerW, innerH) / 2 - leafLabelReserve`. Default `startAngle = -pi/2` so the first leaf sits at 12 o'clock. Per-node `color` always wins; otherwise leaves use `leafColor` and internals use `internalColor`. Leaf labels (`showLeafLabels=true` by default): `rotateLeafLabels=true` (default) rotates each label to the leaf's tangent angle; labels on the bottom half (angle in `(pi/2, 3pi/2)`) are flipped 180 deg to keep text upright; anchor flips to `end` accordingly. `rotateLeafLabels=false` falls back to absolute outside-the-leaf placement with text-anchor based on `cos(angle)`. Internal labels hidden by default; `showInternalLabels=true` renders them above the internal node centroid. Hover/focus on a node opens a tooltip with label, depth, and either `leaf` (for leaves) or `<leafCount> leaves` (for internal nodes); hover/focus on a link opens a link tooltip showing `<source> -> <target>` only when no node is also hovered. Per-node + per-link click handlers fire with full payloads. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per node + link (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `root: ChartTreeRadialNode \| null` ({id, label, color?, children?}) / `width?` (420) / `height?` (420) / `padding?` (32) / `leafLabelReserve?` (60) / `startAngle?` (-pi/2) / `linkStyle?` ('curve'\|'elbow'\|'line'; default 'curve') / `nodeRadius?` (3) / `leafRadius?` (4) / `labelGap?` (6) / `leafColor?` / `internalColor?` / `linkColor?` / `showLeafLabels?` (true) / `showInternalLabels?` (false) / `showNodes?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `rotateLeafLabels?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Radial tree') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatLabel?` / `onNodeClick?({node})` / `onLinkClick?({link})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_TREE_RADIAL_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/LEAF_LABEL_RESERVE/NODE_RADIUS/LEAF_RADIUS/LABEL_GAP/START_ANGLE/LINK_COLOR/LEAF_COLOR/INTERNAL_COLOR/LINK_STYLE`; `polarToCartesian(cx, cy, r, angle)` -- standard SVG y-down; `getTreeRadialDefaultColor(isLeaf, leafColor, internalColor)` -- leaf vs internal pick; `flattenTreeRadialHierarchy(root)` -- depth-first flatten returning `{ id, label, depth, parentId, path, isLeaf, color? }[]`; null -> []; `getTreeRadialLeaves(root)` -- filtered leaves in DFS order; `getTreeRadialMaxDepth(flat)` -- deepest depth; `buildTreeRadialLinkPath(source, target, cx, cy, style)` -- canonical link path per style; `computeTreeRadialLayout({root, centerX, centerY, outerRadius, startAngle, linkStyle, leafColor, internalColor})` -- canonical layout returning `{ nodes, links, flat, leafCount, maxDepth, outerRadius, centerX, centerY }`; null / non-positive radius -> empty; `describeTreeRadialChart(root)` -- ARIA summary "Radial tree with N nodes, L leaves, depth D."; null -> "No data". | 11.488 | UI: chart-cluster primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.506 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-cluster.tsx` ships `<ChartCluster>` -- pure-SVG **cluster dendrogram**, sibling of `<ChartDendrogram>` (11.486). Distinct from the plain dendrogram in three ways: (1) **distance-aware depth axis** -- each node carries an optional `distance` (the merge distance in hierarchical clustering); the depth axis encodes distance rather than uniform depth steps. Leaves sit at distance 0; internal nodes sit at their merge distance. (2) **cluster cut line** -- optional `cutDistance` prop draws a horizontal threshold line; every internal node at or below the cut becomes a *cluster root* and its descendants share a colour from the cluster palette. (3) **distance axis with ticks** -- a vertical axis on the left side shows tick marks at evenly-spaced distance values so adopters can read merge heights directly. Distance resolution (`getClusterNodeDistance`): explicit `distance >= 0` always wins. For leaves without an explicit distance, the default is 0. For internal nodes without an explicit distance, the fallback is `(maxDepth - depth) / maxDepth` so the tree visually mimics a uniform-spacing dendrogram in the absence of true cluster heights. Layout (`computeClusterLayout`): leaves laid evenly along the x axis at `leafIndex * (innerW / (leafCount - 1))`; each internal node's x is the *mean* of its children's x positions; y derived from distance with leaves at `padY + innerH` and internal nodes at `padY + innerH - (distance / maxDistance) * innerH`. Links are right-angle elbows: horizontal from parent x to child x at parent's y, then vertical down to child's y -- the canonical cluster dendrogram style that visually distinguishes vertical drops at merge heights. Cluster cut: when `cutDistance > 0` is supplied, walks the tree and marks every internal node with `distance <= cutDistance` as a cluster root; descendants of that root share the cluster id; each cluster id gets its own colour from the 10-color palette (modulo wrap); nodes above the cut keep their default leaf / internal colour; a dashed horizontal cut line + label render at `y(cutDistance)` when `showCutLine=true`. Distance axis (`showDistanceAxis=true` by default): vertical axis on the left at `padX + axisReserve` with evenly-spaced ticks from 0 to `maxDistance`. Leaf labels render rotated 45 deg below each leaf so long labels don't overlap on a dense axis. Hover/focus on a node opens a tooltip with the label, distance, leaf / leafCount, and the cluster id when one is assigned; hover/focus on a link opens a link tooltip. Per-node + per-link click handlers fire with full payloads. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per node + link (suppressed via `animate=false`). | 11.489 | UI: chart-radial-stacked-bar primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.507 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-radial-stacked-bar.tsx` ships `<ChartRadialStackedBar>` -- pure-SVG **radial stacked bar** chart. Each category is a concentric ring around the centre; within each ring, the configured series stack **angularly** so the full 2pi of the ring is divided proportionally by each series's value within that category. Distinct from `<ChartRadialBar>` (11.452) which paints one arc per series with value encoding arc length, `<ChartPolarArea>` (11.478) which uses equal-angle wedges with radius encoding value, and `<ChartStackedBar>` (11.468) which is the linear stacked variant: this primitive is the rings-of-stacks variant where each ring shows the categorical breakdown across the visible series. Layout (`computeRadialStackedBarLayout`): one ring per category stacking outward from `innerRadius` to `outerRadius` with `ringGap` between consecutive rings; `ringThickness = (outerRadius - innerRadius - gaps) / N` where N is the category count. Within each ring, visible series fill the full 2pi minus per-segment `padAngle`s; each segment occupies an arc proportional to `value / categoryTotal`. Non-positive / non-finite values produce no segment (skipped from the ring entirely). Hidden series (controlled via `hiddenSeries` + `onHiddenSeriesChange` or uncontrolled via `defaultHiddenSeries`) drop their segments everywhere; the remaining series reproportion to fill the ring. Per-series `color` always wins; otherwise the 10-color palette maps each `seriesIndex` so the same series uses the same colour across every ring. Default `startAngle = -pi/2` so the first series in each ring starts at 12 o'clock. Center disc shows the grand total of all visible segments; an optional `centerLabel` caption renders above the value when supplied. Ring labels render at the ring's midradius for non-empty rings (toggleable via `showRingLabels`). Hover/focus on a segment sets the hovered key (`categoryId::seriesId`) and opens a tooltip with the category + series labels, the formatted value, and the share within the category. Per-segment click handler fires with `{segment}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per segment (suppressed via `animate=false`). Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_RADIAL_STACKED_BAR_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/INNER_RADIUS/RING_GAP/PAD_ANGLE/START_ANGLE/FILL_OPACITY/PALETTE`; `getRadialStackedBarDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; `polarToCartesian(cx, cy, r, angle)` -- standard SVG y-down; `getRadialStackedBarCategoryTotal(values, hiddenIndices)` -- sum of visible positive-finite values; `computeRadialStackedBarLayout({categories, series, hiddenSeries, cx, cy, innerRadius, outerRadius, ringGap, padAngle, startAngle, fallbackColor})` -- canonical layout returning `{ rings, visibleSeriesCount, totalsByCategory, ringThickness, outerRadius }`; each ring is `{ id, index, label, innerRadius, outerRadius, total, segments }`; each segment is `{ categoryId, categoryIndex, seriesId, seriesIndex, value, shareWithinCategory, startAngle, endAngle, midAngle, innerRadius, outerRadius, color, path }`; empty / non-positive outer / outer<=inner -> empty rings; `describeRadialStackedBarChart(categories, series, hidden, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Radial stacked bar chart with N rings and V visible series. | 11.490 | UI: chart-radial-line primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.508 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-radial-line.tsx` ships `<ChartRadialLine>` -- pure-SVG **radial line / spiral plot** for cyclic / periodic time-series data. Two modes: `cyclic` (default; angle encodes position-in-cycle 0..2pi over `cycleLength` samples; radius encodes value; line closes back to start so the cycle is visually obvious -- ideal for hour-of-day / day-of-week / month-of-year periodicity) and `spiral` (angle accumulates continuously over multiple cycles so cycle 1 sample 0 sits at `startAngle + 2pi`, cycle 2 sample 0 at `startAngle + 4pi`, etc.; radius walks outward over the full sample range with weighted combination of value ratio + sample position so even flat input still spirals while values modulate locally; ideal for showing both within-cycle phase and long-term trend across many cycles). Distinct from `<ChartRadialBar>` (11.452, concentric arc bars), `<ChartPolarArea>` (11.478, equal-angle wedges), `<ChartRadar>` (11.445, multi-axis polygon), and `<ChartRadialStackedBar>` (11.489, rings of stacks): this primitive is the polar line variant for periodic data. Layout (`computeRadialLineLayout`): `radiusForValue` for cyclic = `innerRadius + (value/maxValue) * (outerRadius - innerRadius)`; for spiral = `innerRadius + (0.4 * valueRatio + 0.6 * spiralRatio) * radialSpan`. `angleFor` for cyclic = `startAngle + (positionInCycle / cycleLength) * 2pi` (wraps); for spiral = `startAngle + (sampleIndex / cycleLength) * 2pi` (accumulates). Non-finite values break the painted line (path emits a new `M`) and the offending point collapses to inner radius. `closeCyclic=true` (cyclic mode only) appends a line back to the first finite point + a closing `Z` so the cycle is sealed; also exposed as `fillPath` when `showFill=true`. Axis spokes + axis labels: one per `cycleLength` step around the perimeter; labels default to sample index, supply `axisLabels` (length = cycleLength) for human-readable text; `formatAxis` rewrites further. Rings: one concentric dashed ring per non-zero tick value. Hidden series (controlled via `hiddenSeries` + `onHiddenSeriesChange` or uncontrolled via `defaultHiddenSeries`) drop from the output entirely. Hover/focus on a point sets the hovered key (`seriesId::sampleIndex`) and opens a tooltip with series label, position (axis label or `position N`, plus `cycle K` in spiral mode), and formatted value. Per-point click handler fires with `{point, series}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per series group (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `series: readonly ChartRadialLineSeries[]` ({id, label, data: readonly number[], color?}) / `mode?` ('cyclic'\|'spiral'; default 'cyclic') / `cycleLength: number` (required) / `axisLabels?` / `width?` (380) / `height?` (380) / `padding?` (32) / `innerRadius?` (24) / `startAngle?` (-pi/2) / `maxValue?` / `tickCount?` (4) / `strokeWidth?` (1.6) / `pointRadius?` (3) / `fillOpacity?` (0.15) / `gridColor?` ('#e2e8f0') / `axisColor?` ('#cbd5e1') / `hiddenSeries?` / `defaultHiddenSeries?` / `onHiddenSeriesChange?` / `closeCyclic?` (true) / `showFill?` (false) / `showPoints?` (false) / `showRings?` (true) / `showAxisLabels?` (true) / `showSpokes?` (true) / `showLegend?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Radial line chart') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatAxis?` / `legendPlacement?` ('right'\|'bottom', default 'bottom') / `onPointClick?({point, series})` / `onSeriesToggle?({series, hidden})` / `style?`. | 11.491 | UI: chart-radial-area primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.509 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-radial-area.tsx` ships `<ChartRadialArea>` -- pure-SVG **radial area** chart variant where each series is a **closed polygon with a filled interior** in polar coordinates. Two stack modes: **overlay** (default; every series fills from centre out to its value-radius; overlapping fills use `fillOpacity` so multiple series stay legible on top of each other) and **stacked** (per-sample cumulative sums stack radially; each layer paints an annular band between previous cumulative and its own; peak total maps to outerRadius). Two curves: **linear** (default; straight polygon edges between samples) and **cardinal** (closed cubic-bezier smoothing for the classic D3 radial-area look). Distinct from `<ChartRadialLine>` (11.490) which is line-emphasized for cyclic/spiral data with no stacked mode, `<ChartRadar>` (11.445) which is multi-axis polygon for categorical dimensions, `<ChartPolarArea>` (11.478) which uses equal-angle wedges with radius encoding value, and `<ChartRadialStackedBar>` (11.489) which stacks *angularly* within each category ring. Layout (`computeRadialAreaLayout`): `radiusFor(value) = innerRadius + (value / maxValue) * (outerRadius - innerRadius)`, clamped [0, 1]. Overlay: every layer's `innerRadius` is chart's inner radius; `outerRadius` is `radiusFor(value)`. Stacked: per-sample cumulative sums computed left-to-right across visible series; each layer occupies the annulus from `radiusFor(cumulativeBefore)` to `radiusFor(cumulativeAfter)`; hidden series pause the cumulative cursor. Non-finite / non-positive values clamp to 0 so the layer never inverts. Path building (`buildRadialAreaClosedPath`): overlay (inner ring collapses to a point) emits a single closed M..Z ring for each series; stacked (distinct inner ring) emits two closed rings (outer + reversed inner) with `fillRule="evenodd"` so the SVG paints only the annulus. `linear` uses straight L between samples; `cardinal` uses Catmull-Rom-to-cubic-Bezier on the closed loop. Axis spokes + axis labels one per `cycleLength` step around the perimeter; labels default to sample index; `axisLabels` prop + `formatAxis` rewrite. Rings: one concentric dashed ring per non-zero tick value. Hidden series (controlled `hiddenSeries` + `onHiddenSeriesChange` or uncontrolled `defaultHiddenSeries`) drop from layout; cumulative cursor pauses for hidden layers in stacked mode. Hover/focus on a series group sets the hovered id, dims every other series to opacity 0.4, and opens a tooltip with the series label, sum of finite sample values, and sample count. Per-series click handler fires with `{series}`. Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` per series group (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `series: readonly ChartRadialAreaSeries[]` ({id, label, data: readonly number[], color?}) / `cycleLength: number` (required) / `stackMode?` ('overlay'\|'stacked'; default 'overlay') / `curve?` ('linear'\|'cardinal'; default 'linear') / `axisLabels?` / `width?` (380) / `height?` (380) / `padding?` (32) / `innerRadius?` (24) / `startAngle?` (-pi/2) / `maxValue?` / `tickCount?` (4) / `strokeWidth?` (1.2) / `fillOpacity?` (0.55) / `gridColor?` ('#e2e8f0') / `axisColor?` ('#cbd5e1') / `hiddenSeries?` / `defaultHiddenSeries?` / `onHiddenSeriesChange?` / `showOutline?` (true) / `showRings?` (true) / `showAxisLabels?` (true) / `showSpokes?` (true) / `showLegend?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Radial area chart') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatAxis?` / `legendPlacement?` ('right'\|'bottom', default 'bottom') / `onSeriesClick?({series})` / `onSeriesToggle?({series, hidden})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_RADIAL_AREA_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/INNER_RADIUS/START_ANGLE/TICK_COUNT/STROKE_WIDTH/FILL_OPACITY/GRID_COLOR/AXIS_COLOR/STACK_MODE/CURVE/PALETTE`; `getRadialAreaDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; `polarToCartesian(cx, cy, r, angle)`; `getRadialAreaAngle(pos, cycleLength, startAngle)`; `getRadialAreaSampleCount(series, hidden)` -- longest visible data length; `getRadialAreaMaxValue(series, hidden, stackMode)` -- overlay = largest single value; stacked = largest column sum; empty / all-hidden -> 1; `getRadialAreaTicks(max, count?)` -- non-positive -> [0]; `buildRadialAreaClosedPath(outerPoints, innerPoints, curve)` -- canonical closed path builder; overlay returns single closed ring; stacked returns two closed rings for even-odd fill; cardinal emits C commands; `computeRadialAreaLayout({series, hidden, cycleLength, stackMode, curve, axisLabels?, cx, cy, innerRadius, outerRadius, startAngle, maxValueOverride?, tickCount})` -- canonical layout returning `{ series, axisAngles, rings, maxValue, cycleLength, innerRadius, outerRadius, stackMode }`; empty / non-positive radius / non-positive cycle -> empty; `describeRadialAreaChart(series, hidden, stackMode, cycleLength, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Radial area chart (<stackMode>) with N series, cycle length L, peak value <peak>."; empty / all-hidden / non-positive cycle -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-radial-area-aria-desc"` span; per-outline `<path role="graphics-symbol" tabIndex={0}>` with aria-label `"<label>: <N> samples"`. data-section on every node (chart-radial-area / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -rings / -ring / -spokes / -spoke / -axis-labels / -axis-label / -series / -series-group / -fill / -outline / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-total / -tooltip-samples / -legend / -legend-item / -legend-button / -legend-swatch / -legend-label); root mirrors data-stack-mode, data-curve, data-cycle-length, data-series-count, data-visible-series-count, data-max-value, data-animate; series groups mirror data-series-id, data-series-index, data-series-color, data-series-point-count, data-hovered. 61 vitest cases (1 constants + 1 getRadialAreaDefaultColor + 1 polarToCartesian + 3 getRadialAreaAngle + 2 getRadialAreaSampleCount + 4 getRadialAreaMaxValue + 2 getRadialAreaTicks + 4 buildRadialAreaClosedPath + 13 computeRadialAreaLayout (incl. invariants: overlay starts at innerRadius, stacked layer N inner = layer N-1 outer, stacked peak total maps to outerRadius, non-finite clamp, cardinal emits C) + 2 describeRadialAreaChart + 28 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. | 11.492 | UI: chart-strip primitive | done | SHIPPED v1.11.510 (mgr-direct on c4/c4-mgr-auto). New `web/src/components/ui/chart-strip.tsx` ships `<ChartStrip>` -- pure-SVG one-dimensional **strip plot** (also known as a 1D scatter or strip chart). Each data point gets a small mark (tick line by default or filled circle) placed along a single value axis. Multiple groups stack into parallel lanes; an optional deterministic jitter offsets coincident points in the orthogonal direction so dense regions remain readable. Distinct from `<ChartScatter>` which paints 2D xy points (both axes encode), `<ChartBubble>` (11.470) which is 2D xy with size encoding, `<ChartDotPlot>` which stacks dots vertically by bin to show frequency (Wilkinson dot plot), `<ChartBoxplot>` (11.455) which renders a 5-number summary rather than raw points, `<ChartHistogram>` (11.473) which paints binned counts, `<ChartViolin>` which paints KDE-shaped density envelopes, `<ChartRidge>` (11.474) which stacks density curves across lanes, and `<ChartCalendarHeatmap>` (11.471) which is a 2D day grid coloured by value. Value axis: range auto-derived from finite visible values (collapsed range expands +/- 0.5; empty -> (0..1)); explicit `valueMin` / `valueMax` clamp out-of-range points to the nearest endpoint instead of dropping them. `horizontal` maps the value axis to x (left -> right); `vertical` maps it to y (bottom -> top). Lanes: total inner height (or width, for vertical) is divided into N equal lanes separated by `laneGap` px; lane labels render at the lane's leading edge. Jitter: `getStripJitter(seed, groupIndex, pointIndex)` returns a deterministic value in `[-1, 1]` using a mulberry32-style mixer (`s = seed ^ gi*0x9e3779b1 ^ pi*0x85ebca6b`); final offset = `jitter * (laneHeight/2) * getStripJitter(...)`. Identical input always produces identical output so points never reshuffle across re-renders. Marks: `'tick'` = vertical (horizontal orientation) / horizontal (vertical orientation) line segment of length `markSize` (default 14); `'dot'` = filled circle of radius `markSize` (default 3). Hover/focus on a mark dims every other mark to opacity 0.35 and opens a tooltip with the group label and formatted value. Per-mark click handler fires with `{group, point}`. Legend buttons toggle group visibility (uncontrolled + controlled via `hiddenGroups` / `onHiddenGroupsChange`). Mount fade via `motion-safe:animate-fade-in` (suppressed via `animate=false`). API: `groups: readonly ChartStripGroup[]` ({id, label, values: readonly number[], color?}) / `orientation?` ('horizontal'\|'vertical'; default 'horizontal') / `mark?` ('tick'\|'dot'; default 'tick') / `jitter?` (0) / `jitterSeed?` (1) / `valueMin?` / `valueMax?` / `width?` (560) / `height?` (320) / `padding?` (40) / `laneGap?` (8) / `tickCount?` (5) / `markSize?` / `markOpacity?` (0.65) / `strokeWidth?` (1.2) / `gridColor?` ('#e2e8f0') / `axisColor?` ('#cbd5e1') / `hiddenGroups?` / `defaultHiddenGroups?` / `onHiddenGroupsChange?` / `showAxis?` (true) / `showGrid?` (true) / `showLegend?` (true) / `showLaneLabels?` (true) / `showTooltip?` (true) / `animate?` (true) / `className?` / `ariaLabel?` (default 'Strip plot') / `ariaDescription?` / `formatValue?` / `formatGroup?` / `valueLabel?` / `onPointClick?({group, point})` / `onGroupToggle?({group, hidden})` / `style?`. Pure helpers exported: `DEFAULT_CHART_STRIP_WIDTH/HEIGHT/PADDING/LANE_GAP/TICK_COUNT/MARK_TICK_SIZE/MARK_DOT_SIZE/MARK_OPACITY/STROKE_WIDTH/GRID_COLOR/AXIS_COLOR/ORIENTATION/MARK/JITTER/JITTER_SEED/PALETTE`; `getStripDefaultColor(index)` -- 10-color palette modulo wrap; invalid index -> color 0; `getStripFiniteValues(values)` -- drops non-finite; non-array -> []; `getStripBounds(groups, hidden?)` -- min/max across visible finite values; empty -> (0..1); collapsed +/- 0.5; `getStripTicks(min, max, count?)` -- evenly-spaced; collapsed -> single tick; invalid range -> []; `getStripJitter(seed, gi, pi)` -- deterministic [-1, 1] mulberry32-style mix; `computeStripLayout(input)` -- canonical layout returning `{ groups, ticks, valueMin, valueMax, orientation, mark, innerWidth, innerHeight, laneHeight }`; degenerate canvas / empty groups / all-hidden -> empty; clamps out-of-range values to range endpoints; jitter offsets bounded by `laneHeight/2`; `describeStripChart(groups, hidden?, formatValue?)` -- ARIA summary "Strip plot of N values across M groups, range <min> to <max>."; empty / no finite values -> "No data". ARIA: root `<div role="region">` + `aria-label`, SVG `role="img"` + same `aria-label`, sr-only `data-section="chart-strip-aria-desc"` span; per-mark `<line|circle role="graphics-symbol" tabIndex={0}>` with aria-label `"<group label>: <formatted value>"`. data-section on every node (chart-strip / -canvas / -aria-desc / -svg / -grid / -grid-line / -axes / -axis / -ticks / -tick / -tick-label / -value-label / -lane-labels / -lane-label / -groups / -group / -mark / -tooltip / -tooltip-label / -tooltip-value / -legend / -legend-item / -legend-button / -legend-swatch / -legend-label); root mirrors data-orientation, data-mark, data-jitter, data-group-count, data-visible-group-count, data-finite-count, data-animate; group mirrors data-group-id, data-group-index, data-group-color, data-group-point-count, data-group-finite-count; mark mirrors data-mark-kind, data-group-id, data-point-index, data-value, data-jitter-offset, data-hovered. 67 vitest cases (1 constants + 2 getStripDefaultColor + 2 getStripFiniteValues + 5 getStripBounds + 4 getStripTicks + 3 getStripJitter + 12 computeStripLayout + 4 describeStripChart + 34 component) all pass under vitest 4.1.5. TypeScript clean for touched files. Exported via components/ui barrel. Out of scope (documented in docs/patches/11.492-ui-chart-strip.md): half-eye / mean-bar overlays (host stacks a `<ChartBoxplot>`); beeswarm-style non-overlapping layout (v1 is random jitter, not force-directed); external selection / highlight by id (hover/focus only); log-scale value axis (linear only; host pre-logs); pre-aggregated `{value, count}` input (v1 always one mark per value).
